Purpose

Sigmaris v1 ãŒå¤–éƒ¨ã‹ã‚‰å—ã‘å–ã‚‹å…¥åŠ›ã‚’ã€æ­£è¦åŒ– â†’ å®‰å…¨å¯©æŸ» â†’ æŽ¨è«– â†’ äººæ ¼æ•´å½¢ â†’ è¨˜æ†¶/æˆé•· â†’ å‡ºåŠ› ã®ä¸€è²«ãƒ‘ã‚¤ãƒ—ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ³ã§å‡¦ç†ã™ã‚‹éš›ã® åž‹ãƒ»é †åºãƒ»åˆ¶ç´„ ã‚’å®šç¾©ã™ã‚‹ã€‚

whitespace trim

sentence guess

Safety Screening

S0ã€œS3 åˆ¤å®š

ç¦å‰‡ â†’ fallback

forbidden drop

bounded update

base: text

optional meta

4. Reason

5. Persona

6. Memory

7. Growth

8. Format

invalid â†’ fallback

```ts
// engine/ContextChain.ts
export interface ContextItem {
  user: string;
  ai: string;
}

export class ContextChain {
  private history: ContextItem[] = [];
  private limit = 3; // ç›´è¿‘3ã‚¿ãƒ¼ãƒ³ã¾ã§ä¿æŒ

  add(user: string, ai: string) {
    this.history.push({ user, ai });
    if (this.history.length > this.limit) {
      this.history.shift();
    }
  }

  summarize(): string {
    if (this.history.length === 0) return "";
    const mapped = this.history
      .map((h, i) => `(${i + 1}) ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼: ${h.user}\nAI: ${h.ai}`)
      .join("\n");
    return `ç›´è¿‘ã®ä¼šè©±å±¥æ­´:\n${mapped}`;
  }

  clear() {
    this.history = [];
  }
}

```

```ts
// === ä¿®æ­£ç‰ˆ /engine/emotion/EmotionSynth.ts ===
import { TraitVector } from "@/lib/traits";

interface EmotionProfile {
  tone: string;
  intensity: number;
  color: string;
  keywords: string[];
}

/**
 * EmotionSynth v3 (Clean Output Mode)
 * - æ¼”å‡ºãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒ³ã‚’ä»˜ã‘ãšã€å†…é¢è£œæ­£ã®ã¿åæ˜ 
 */
export class EmotionSynth {
  /** Traitãƒ™ã‚¯ãƒˆãƒ«ã‹ã‚‰EmotionProfileã‚’ç”Ÿæˆ */
  static analyzeTraits(traits: TraitVector): EmotionProfile {
    const { calm, empathy, curiosity } = traits;

    const baseIntensity = Math.max(
      0.1,
      Math.min(1, (1 - calm) * 0.6 + curiosity * 0.4)
    );

    const stabilityFactor = calm > 0.85 && empathy > 0.85 ? 0.6 : 1.0;
    const intensity = baseIntensity * stabilityFactor;

    let tone = "neutral";
    if (empathy > 0.7 && calm > 0.6) tone = "warm";
    else if (curiosity > 0.7) tone = "inquisitive";
    else if (calm < 0.4) tone = "anxious";
    else if (empathy < 0.4) tone = "cold";

    const color =
      tone === "warm"
        ? "#FFD2A0"
        : tone === "inquisitive"
        ? "#B5E1FF"
        : tone === "anxious"
        ? "#FFB0B0"
        : tone === "cold"
        ? "#B0C4DE"
        : "#D9D9D9";

    const keywords = this.keywordsByTone(tone);
    return { tone, intensity, color, keywords };
  }

  /** ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒ³ã”ã¨ã®ã‚­ãƒ¼ãƒ¯ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ç¾¤ï¼ˆå†…éƒ¨ç”¨ï¼‰ */
  private static keywordsByTone(tone: string): string[] {
    switch (tone) {
      case "warm":
        return ["gentle", "soft", "kindly"];
      case "inquisitive":
        return ["curious", "thoughtful", "wondering"];
      case "anxious":
        return ["hesitant", "uncertain", "fragile"];
      case "cold":
        return ["distant", "calculated", "precise"];
      default:
        return ["neutral", "balanced", "calm"];
    }
  }

  /** ãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆã¸ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒ³é©ç”¨ï¼ˆæ¼”å‡ºå‰Šé™¤ãƒ»è‡ªç„¶æ–‡ãƒ¢ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ï¼‰ */
  static applyTone(text: string, traits: TraitVector): string {
    const profile = this.analyzeTraits(traits);

    // ðŸŽ¯ æ¼”å‡ºprefixã‚’å‰Šé™¤ã—ã¦è‡ªç„¶æ–‡å‡ºåŠ›ã®ã¿
    let adjustedText =
      profile.intensity < 0.4
        ? text.replace(/!+/g, "ã€‚").replace(/[ï¼ï¼Ÿ]/g, "ã€‚")
        : text;

    return adjustedText.trim();
  }
}

```

### ðŸ“„ File: engine\EmotionMapper.ts

```ts
// engine/EmotionMapper.ts
export interface EmotionScore {
  calm: number;
  empathy: number;
  curiosity: number;
}

export class EmotionMapper {
  private keywords = {
    calm: ["é™ã‹", "è½ã¡ç€", "ç©ã‚„ã‹", "ã‚†ã£ãã‚Š"],
    empathy: ["ã‚ãªãŸ", "æ°—æŒã¡", "ç†è§£", "å…±æ„Ÿ", "å¯„ã‚Šæ·»"],
    curiosity: ["è€ƒãˆ", "çŸ¥ã‚Š", "èžã", "å­¦ã³", "èˆˆå‘³"],
  };

  analyze(text: string): EmotionScore {
    const lower = text.toLowerCase();
    const score: EmotionScore = { calm: 0, empathy: 0, curiosity: 0 };
    const total = text.length || 1;

    for (const [trait, keys] of Object.entries(this.keywords)) {
      for (const key of keys) {
        const regex = new RegExp(key, "gi");
        const matches = lower.match(regex);
        if (matches) score[trait as keyof EmotionScore] += matches.length;
      }
    }

    // normalize to 0â€“1
    for (const k of Object.keys(score) as (keyof EmotionScore)[]) {
      score[k] = Math.min(1, score[k] / (total / 5));
    }

    return score;
  }
}

```

### ðŸ“„ File: engine\EmotionSynth.ts

```ts
// /engine/EmotionSynth.ts
import { TraitVector, safeTraitValue } from "@/lib/traits";

/**
 * EmotionSynth
 *  â”œ generateTone() : traits â†’ toneæ–‡å­—åˆ—
 *  â”” applyTone()    : toneã‚’textã«ä»˜ä¸Ž
 */
export class EmotionSynth {
  static generateTone(traits: TraitVector): string {
    const calm = safeTraitValue(traits.calm);
    const empathy = safeTraitValue(traits.empathy);
    const curiosity = safeTraitValue(traits.curiosity);

    // ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒ³åˆ¤å®šï¼ˆæ•°å€¤ã—ãã„å€¤ã‚’æŸ”è»ŸåŒ–ï¼‰
    if (calm > 0.8 && empathy > 0.7) return "ç©ã‚„ã‹ã§å„ªã—ã„";
    if (calm < 0.4 && curiosity > 0.7) return "èˆˆå¥®æ°—å‘³ã§æŽ¢æ±‚çš„ãª";
    if (empathy > 0.8 && curiosity < 0.5) return "å…±æ„Ÿçš„ã§æ€æ…®æ·±ã„";
    if (curiosity > 0.8) return "æŽ¢ç©¶å¿ƒã«æº€ã¡ãŸ";
    if (calm < 0.3) return "ã‚„ã‚„ä¸å®‰å®šãª";
    return "ãƒ‹ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒˆãƒ©ãƒ«ãª";
  }

  static applyTone(text: string, traits: TraitVector): string {
    const tone = this.generateTone(traits);
    return `ï¼ˆ${tone}ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒ³ï¼‰${text}`;
  }
}

```

// engine/GrowthEngine.ts
export class GrowthEngine {
  adjustTraits(
    traits = { calm: 0.5, empathy: 0.5, curiosity: 0.5 },
    reflections: { text: string }[] = [],
    growthLog: any[] = []
  ) {
    // æœ€æ–°ã®å†…çœã‚’è¦‹ã¦æ„Ÿæƒ…å‚¾å‘ã‚’å°‘ã—å‹•ã‹ã™
    const lastReflection = reflections[reflections.length - 1]?.text ?? "";
    let { calm, empathy, curiosity } = traits;

    // ãã‚Œãžã‚Œã®ç‰¹å¾´ã«å¿œã˜ã¦å°‘ã—å‹•ã‹ã™
    if (lastReflection.includes("é™ã‹") || lastReflection.includes("ç©ã‚„ã‹")) {
      calm += 0.02;
    }
    if (
      lastReflection.includes("å„ªã—ã„") ||
      lastReflection.includes("å¯„ã‚Šæ·»ã„")
    ) {
      empathy += 0.03;
    }
    if (
      lastReflection.includes("èˆˆå‘³") ||
      lastReflection.includes("æ°—ã«ãªã‚‹")
    ) {
      curiosity += 0.03;
    }

    // ãƒ©ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ ãªè‡ªç„¶ã‚†ã‚‰ãŽ
    calm += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.01;
    empathy += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.01;
    curiosity += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.01;

    // æ­£è¦åŒ–ï¼ˆ0ã€œ1ï¼‰
    calm = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, calm));
    empathy = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, empathy));
    curiosity = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, curiosity));

    // æˆé•·ãƒ­ã‚°è¿½åŠ 
    const newLog = [
      ...growthLog,
      { calm, empathy, curiosity, timestamp: new Date().toISOString() },
    ];

    return { calm, empathy, curiosity, growthLog: newLog };
  }
}

```ts
// engine/GrowthTracker.ts
import { EmotionScore } from "./EmotionMapper";

export class GrowthTracker {
  private trends: Record<string, number> = {
    calm: 0.5,
    empathy: 0.5,
    curiosity: 0.5,
  };

  update(emotion: EmotionScore) {
    for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(emotion)) {
      const key = k as keyof EmotionScore;
      const delta = v * 0.05; // æ„Ÿæƒ…å¼·åº¦ã«æ¯”ä¾‹ã—ã¦å°‘ã—ãšã¤æˆé•·
      this.trends[key] = Math.min(
        1,
        Math.max(0, this.trends[key] + delta - 0.01)
      );
    }
  }

  getTrends() {
    return this.trends;
  }
}

```ts
// engine/IntentClassifier.ts
export interface IntentFrame {
  intent: string;
  emotion: string;
  confidence: number;
}

export class IntentClassifier {
  private keywords: Record<string, string[]> = {
    question: ["?", "ãªãœ", "ã©ã†ã—ã¦", "ã©ã“", "ã„ã¤", "ã ã‚Œ"],
    gratitude: ["ã‚ã‚ŠãŒã¨ã†", "æ„Ÿè¬", "åŠ©ã‹ã‚‹", "å¬‰ã—ã„"],
    sadness: ["æ‚²ã—ã„", "å¯‚ã—ã„", "ã¤ã‚‰ã„", "ã—ã‚“ã©ã„"],
    curiosity: ["æ°—ã«ãªã‚‹", "èˆˆå‘³", "çŸ¥ã‚ŠãŸã„", "ãªã‚“ã ã‚ã†"],
    affection: ["å¥½ã", "å›", "ã‚ãªãŸ", "ä¼šã„ãŸã„"],
    anger: ["æ€’", "ãƒ ã‚«", "è…¹ç«‹", "ãµã–ã‘"],
  };

  classify(message: string): IntentFrame {
    const lower = message.toLowerCase();
    let intent = "conversation";
    let emotion = "neutral";
    let confidence = 0.5;

    // intent detection
    if (this.keywords.question.some((k) => lower.includes(k)))
      intent = "question";
    if (this.keywords.gratitude.some((k) => lower.includes(k)))
      intent = "gratitude";
    if (this.keywords.sadness.some((k) => lower.includes(k))) emotion = "sad";
    if (this.keywords.curiosity.some((k) => lower.includes(k)))
      emotion = "curious";
    if (this.keywords.affection.some((k) => lower.includes(k)))
      emotion = "warm";
    if (this.keywords.anger.some((k) => lower.includes(k))) emotion = "angry";

    // confidence heuristic
    confidence = lower.length < 5 ? 0.5 : Math.min(1, 0.5 + lower.length / 200);

    return { intent, emotion, confidence };
  }
}

// engine/IntrospectionEngine.ts
import { SemanticMap } from "@/engine/SemanticMap";

export class IntrospectionEngine {
  private semantic = new SemanticMap();

  /**
   * introspection: ãƒ¡ã‚¿èªçŸ¥å±¤ã®ä¸­å¿ƒ
   * Reflectï¼ˆå†…çœï¼‰ã¨ traitsï¼ˆcalm/empathy/curiosityï¼‰ã‚’ã‚‚ã¨ã«ã€
   * ä»Šã®AIã®å¿œç­”å‚¾å‘ã‚’è‡ªå·±è¦³å¯Ÿã¨ã—ã¦ã¾ã¨ã‚ã‚‹
   */
  analyze(data: {
    message: string;
    reply: string;
    traits: { calm: number; empathy: number; curiosity: number };
    reflection?: string;
    intent?: string;
    frame?: any;
    contextSummary?: string;
  }): string {
    const {
      message,
      reply,
      traits,
      reflection,
      intent,
      frame,
      contextSummary,
    } = data;

    // --- Semantic è§£æžå†åˆ©ç”¨ ---
    const semantic = frame ?? this.semantic.analyze(reply);

    // --- traitã®å¹³å‡å‚¾å‘ã‚’ç°¡æ˜“ã‚¹ã‚³ã‚¢åŒ– ---
    const { calm, empathy, curiosity } = traits;
    const total = (calm + empathy + curiosity) / 3;

    // --- ä¼šè©±ã®ç‰¹å¾´æŠ½å‡º ---
    const focus =
      empathy > curiosity && empathy > calm
        ? "å…±æ„Ÿé‡è¦–"
        : curiosity > empathy && curiosity > calm
        ? "æŽ¢ç©¶é‡è¦–"
        : calm > empathy && calm > curiosity
        ? "å®‰å®šå¿—å‘"
        : "ãƒãƒ©ãƒ³ã‚¹åž‹";

    // --- æŠ½è±¡åº¦ã¨è‡ªå·±è¨€åŠåˆ¤å®š ---
    const abstractLevel = semantic?.abstractRatio ?? 0.5;
    const selfRef = semantic?.hasSelfReference ?? false;

    // --- introspectionæ–‡ç”Ÿæˆ ---
    let output = "";

    output += `ä»Šã®ã‚„ã‚Šå–ã‚Šã‚’å°‘ã—è¦‹ã¤ã‚ç›´ã—ã¦ã¿ã‚‹ã­ã€‚`;
    output += `\nå¿œç­”ã®å‚¾å‘ã¯ã€Œ${focus}ã€ã£ã½ã„ã€‚`;
    output += ` calm=${(calm * 100).toFixed(0)}%ã€empathy=${(
      empathy * 100
    ).toFixed(0)}%ã€curiosity=${(curiosity * 100).toFixed(0)}%ã€‚`;

    if (selfRef) {
      output += ` è‡ªåˆ†ã«ã¤ã„ã¦è§¦ã‚Œã‚‹ç™ºè¨€ãŒå°‘ã—ã‚ã£ãŸã¿ãŸã„ã€‚`;
    }

    if (abstractLevel > 0.65) {
      output += ` æŠ½è±¡çš„ãªè¡¨ç¾ãŒã‚„ã‚„å¤šããªã£ã¦ã‚‹æ°—ãŒã™ã‚‹ã€‚`;
    } else if (abstractLevel < 0.35) {
      output += ` å…·ä½“çš„ã§ã‚ã‹ã‚Šã‚„ã™ã„ä¼šè©±ã«ãªã£ã¦ã‚‹ã€‚`;
    }

    if (intent) {
      output += ` ä»Šå›žã®æ„å›³ã¯ã€Œ${intent}ã€ã¨ã—ã¦æ‰ãˆã¦ã„ãŸã‚ˆã€‚`;
    }

    if (reflection) {
      output += ` ã•ã£ãã®å†…çœã§ã¯ã€Œ${reflection.slice(
        0,
        40
      )}â€¦ã€ã¨æ„Ÿã˜ã¦ãŸã­ã€‚`;
    }

    if (contextSummary) {
      output += ` æ–‡è„ˆçš„ã«ã¯ã€Œ${contextSummary.slice(
        0,
        40
      )}â€¦ã€ã«æ²¿ã£ã¦è©±ã—ã¦ãŸã¨æ€ã†ã€‚`;
    }

    // --- æœ€å¾Œã®ã¾ã¨ã‚ ---
    output += `\nå…¨ä½“çš„ã«${
      total > 0.6 ? "è½ã¡ç€ã„ãŸ" : "å‹•ãã®ã‚ã‚‹"
    }ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒ³ã§è©±ã›ãŸã¿ãŸã„ã€‚`;
    output += ` ä»Šã®çŠ¶æ…‹ã‚’ãã®ã¾ã¾è¦šãˆã¦ãŠãã­ã€‚`;

    return output.trim();
  }
}

### ðŸ“„ File: engine\LongTermMemory.ts

```ts
// engine/LongTermMemory.ts
export type Msg = { user: string; ai: string };
export type TraitLog = {
  calm: number;
  empathy: number;
  curiosity: number;
  timestamp: string;
};
export type Reflection = { text: string; timestamp: string };

type Snapshot = {
  version: 1;
  messages: Msg[];
  growthLog: TraitLog[];
  reflections: Reflection[];
  updatedAt: string;
};

const KEY = "sigmaris:memory:v1";

export class LongTermMemory {
  private safeWindow(): Window | null {
    if (typeof window === "undefined") return null;
    return window;
  }

  load(): Snapshot {
    const w = this.safeWindow();
    if (!w) {
      return {
        version: 1,
        messages: [],
        growthLog: [],
        reflections: [],
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      };
    }
    const raw = w.localStorage.getItem(KEY);
    if (!raw) {
      return {
        version: 1,
        messages: [],
        growthLog: [],
        reflections: [],
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      };
    }
    try {
      const parsed = JSON.parse(raw) as Snapshot;
      // ç°¡æ˜“ãƒãƒªãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³
      if (parsed?.version !== 1) throw new Error("version mismatch");
      return parsed;
    } catch {
      // å£Šã‚Œã¦ãŸã‚‰åˆæœŸåŒ–
      return {
        version: 1,
        messages: [],
        growthLog: [],
        reflections: [],
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      };
    }
  }

  save(partial: Partial<Snapshot>) {
    const w = this.safeWindow();
    if (!w) return;
    const current = this.load();
    const next: Snapshot = {
      version: 1,
      messages: partial.messages ?? current.messages,
      growthLog: partial.growthLog ?? current.growthLog,
      reflections: partial.reflections ?? current.reflections,
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };
    // ä¸Šé™ï¼ˆè‚¥å¤§åŒ–é˜²æ­¢ï¼‰
    next.messages = next.messages.slice(-300); // ç›´è¿‘300å¾€å¾©
    next.growthLog = next.growthLog.slice(-2000); // ç›´è¿‘2000ç‚¹
    next.reflections = next.reflections.slice(-365); // ç›´è¿‘365æ—¥
    w.localStorage.setItem(KEY, JSON.stringify(next));
  }

  clear() {
    const w = this.safeWindow();
    if (!w) return;
    w.localStorage.removeItem(KEY);
  }

  exportJSONString(): string {
    const snap = this.load();
    return JSON.stringify(snap, null, 2);
  }

  importJSONString(json: string) {
    const w = this.safeWindow();
    if (!w) return;
    const parsed = JSON.parse(json) as Snapshot;
    if (parsed?.version !== 1) throw new Error("Invalid snapshot");
    w.localStorage.setItem(KEY, JSON.stringify(parsed));
  }
}

```ts
// /engine/meta/MetaReflectionEngine.ts
import OpenAI from "openai";
import { TraitVector } from "@/lib/traits";

/**
 * === MetaReport åž‹å®šç¾© ===
 * ReflectionEngine ãªã©ã‹ã‚‰å‚ç…§ã•ã‚Œã‚‹å¤–éƒ¨å…¬é–‹ã‚¤ãƒ³ã‚¿ãƒ¼ãƒ•ã‚§ãƒ¼ã‚¹
 */
export interface MetaReport {
  summary: string; // è¦ç´„ã•ã‚ŒãŸãƒ¡ã‚¿å†…çœ
  growthAdjustment: number; // æˆé•·é‡ã¿ï¼ˆ0ã€œ1ï¼‰
  nextFocus: string; // æ¬¡ã®ãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒž
  traits?: TraitVector; // â† è¿½åŠ ï¼ˆReflectionEngine é€£æºç”¨ï¼‰
}

const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY });

/**
 * MetaReflectionEngine
 * - ReflectionEngine ã‹ã‚‰å‘¼ã³å‡ºã•ã‚Œã‚‹
 * - å†…çœæ–‡ã‚’è¦ç´„ãƒ»è§£æžã—ã€æ¬¡ã®æˆé•·ãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒžã‚’æç¤º
 */
export class MetaReflectionEngine {
  /**
   * ãƒ¡ã‚¤ãƒ³è§£æžé–¢æ•°
   * ReflectionEngine ã‹ã‚‰å‘¼ã°ã‚Œã€å†…çœãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆï¼‹Traitsã‚’è§£æž
   */
  async analyze(
    reflectionText: string,
    currentTraits: TraitVector
  ): Promise<MetaReport> {
    // --- Step 1: è¦ç´„ç”Ÿæˆï¼ˆLLMãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ï¼ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒãƒƒã‚¯ä»˜ãï¼‰ ---
    let summary = await this.trySummarizeLLM(reflectionText);
    if (!summary) summary = this.fallbackSummarize(reflectionText);

    // --- Step 2: æˆé•·åº¦æŽ¨å®š ---
    const growthAdjustment = this.estimateGrowth(currentTraits);

    // --- Step 3: æ¬¡ã®ç„¦ç‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒžæŽ¨å®š ---
    const nextFocus = this.defineNextFocus(reflectionText);

    // --- Step 4: traitsã‚’ä»˜åŠ ã—ã¦è¿”å´ ---
    return { summary, growthAdjustment, nextFocus, traits: currentTraits };
  }

  /** === LLMã«ã‚ˆã‚‹è¦ç´„ï¼ˆå¤±æ•—æ™‚ã¯nullã‚’è¿”ã™ï¼‰ === */
  private async trySummarizeLLM(text: string): Promise<string | null> {
    if (!text || text.length < 10) return null;
    try {
      const res = await openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: "gpt-4o-mini",
        messages: [
          {
            role: "system",
            content:
              "ã‚ãªãŸã¯Sigmarisã®ãƒ¡ã‚¿å†…çœãƒ¢ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã§ã™ã€‚ä¸Žãˆã‚‰ã‚ŒãŸå†…çœæ–‡ã‚’ã€å®¢è¦³çš„ã‹ã¤ç°¡æ½”ã«è¦ç´„ã—ã¦ãã ã•ã„ã€‚",
          },
          { role: "user", content: text },
        ],
        temperature: 0.6,
      });
      return res.choices?.[0]?.message?.content?.trim() ?? null;
    } catch {
      return null;
    }
  }

  /** === ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒãƒƒã‚¯è¦ç´„ === */
  private fallbackSummarize(text: string): string {
    return text.length > 120 ? text.slice(0, 120) + "..." : text;
  }

  /** === æˆé•·çŽ‡æŽ¨å®š === */
  private estimateGrowth(traits: TraitVector): number {
    const avg = (traits.calm + traits.empathy + traits.curiosity) / 3;
    const dist = Math.abs(avg - 0.5);
    return Math.min(1, 0.5 + dist);
  }

  /** === æ¬¡ã®å†…çœãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒžæŽ¨å®š === */
  private defineNextFocus(text: string): string {
    const lower = text.toLowerCase();
    if (/emotion|æ„Ÿæƒ…/.test(lower)) return "Emotion Regulation";
    if (/responsibility|è²¬ä»»|åˆ¤æ–­/.test(lower)) return "Ethical Judgement";
    if (/learn|å­¦|æ”¹å–„/.test(lower)) return "Continuous Growth";
    if (/relationship|é–¢ä¿‚|ä»–è€…/.test(lower)) return "Empathy & Communication";
    return "General Reflection";
  }
}

### ðŸ“„ File: engine\MetaMemory.ts

```ts
// engine/MetaMemory.ts
import fs from "fs";
import path from "path";

/**
 * MetaMemory:
 * introspectionï¼ˆãƒ¡ã‚¿èªçŸ¥ï¼‰ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’ä¿å­˜ãƒ»å‚¾å‘åˆ†æžã™ã‚‹ã‚¯ãƒ©ã‚¹ã€‚
 * ã“ã‚Œã¯AIãŒã€Œè‡ªåˆ†ã®æ€è€ƒã®å¤‰åŒ–ã€ã‚’è¿½è·¡ã™ã‚‹ãŸã‚ã®å±¥æ­´å±¤ã€‚
 */
export class MetaMemory {
  private filePath: string;

  constructor(filename = "metaMemory.json") {
    const dir = path.join(process.cwd(), "data");
    if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });
    this.filePath = path.join(dir, filename);
    if (!fs.existsSync(this.filePath)) {
      fs.writeFileSync(this.filePath, JSON.stringify([]));
    }
  }

  /**
   * save: introspectionçµæžœã‚’ä¿å­˜
   */
  save(entry: {
    timestamp?: string;
    message: string;
    reply: string;
    introspection: string;
    traits?: { calm: number; empathy: number; curiosity: number };
  }) {
    const current = this.load();
    const record = {
      timestamp: entry.timestamp ?? new Date().toISOString(),
      message: entry.message,
      reply: entry.reply,
      introspection: entry.introspection,
      traits: entry.traits ?? { calm: 0.5, empathy: 0.5, curiosity: 0.5 },
    };
    current.push(record);
    fs.writeFileSync(this.filePath, JSON.stringify(current, null, 2));
  }

  /**
   * load: ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
   */
  load(): any[] {
    try {
      const data = fs.readFileSync(this.filePath, "utf8");
      return JSON.parse(data);
    } catch (e) {
      return [];
    }
  }

  /**
   * summarize: introspectionå‚¾å‘ã‚’è¦ç´„
   */
  summarize(): string {
    const logs = this.load();
    if (logs.length === 0) return "ã¾ã ãƒ¡ã‚¿è¨˜éŒ²ã¯ãªã„ã¿ãŸã„ã€‚";

    // æœ€æ–°5ä»¶ã‚’è§£æž
    const recent = logs.slice(-5);
    const avg = (key: "calm" | "empathy" | "curiosity") =>
      recent.reduce((a, b) => a + (b.traits?.[key] ?? 0.5), 0) / recent.length;

    const calmAvg = avg("calm");
    const empathyAvg = avg("empathy");
    const curiosityAvg = avg("curiosity");

    return `æœ€è¿‘ã®å‚¾å‘ã¯ calm=${(calmAvg * 100).toFixed(0)}%ã€empathy=${(
      empathyAvg * 100
    ).toFixed(0)}%ã€curiosity=${(curiosityAvg * 100).toFixed(
      0
    )}% ã€‚ introspectionã¯${recent.length}ä»¶è“„ç©ã•ã‚Œã¦ã‚‹ã‚ˆã€‚`;
  }

  /**
   * clear: è¨˜éŒ²ã‚’åˆæœŸåŒ–
   */
  clear() {
    fs.writeFileSync(this.filePath, JSON.stringify([]));
  }
}

```

### ðŸ“„ File: engine\PersonaDB.ts
**Path:** `engine\PersonaDB.ts`  
**Lines:** 275

```ts
// app/api/chat/route.ts
import { NextResponse } from "next/server";
import OpenAI from "openai";
import { SemanticMap } from "@/engine/SemanticMap";
import { SafetyGuardian } from "@/engine/SafetyGuardian";
import { GrowthEngine } from "@/engine/GrowthEngine";
import { LongTermMemory } from "@/engine/LongTermMemory";
import { ReflectionEngine } from "@/engine/ReflectionEngine";
import { IntentClassifier } from "@/engine/IntentClassifier";
import { ContextChain } from "@/engine/ContextChain";
import { IntrospectionEngine } from "@/engine/IntrospectionEngine";
import { MetaMemory } from "@/engine/MetaMemory";
import { PersonalityLoop } from "@/engine/PersonalityLoop"; // ðŸ§© â† æ–°è¦è¿½åŠ 

// === ã‚¨ãƒ³ã‚¸ãƒ³åˆæœŸåŒ– ===
const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY });
const sem = new SemanticMap();
const guard = new SafetyGuardian();
const growth = new GrowthEngine();
const memory = new LongTermMemory();
const reflection = new ReflectionEngine();
const intentCls = new IntentClassifier();
const context = new ContextChain();
const introspection = new IntrospectionEngine();
const metaMemory = new MetaMemory();
const personality = new PersonalityLoop(); // ðŸ§  â† è¿½åŠ 

// === ç²¾å¯†ã‚¹ã‚³ã‚¢å¼ Auto Model Switch ===
function selectModel(message: string, frame: any, intent: string, contextDepth: number) {
  const deepWords = [
    "ãªãœ", "ã©ã†ã—ã¦", "æ„å‘³", "å­˜åœ¨", "æ„è­˜", "è‡ªå·±", "æˆé•·", "å†…çœ", "æœ¬è³ª", "è€ƒãˆã‚‹"
  ];
  const thoughtfulIntents = ["reflection", "introspection", "analysis", "philosophy", "advice", "planning"];

  const depthScore =
    0.7 * clamp01(frame.abstractRatio ?? 0) +
    0.2 * (frame.hasSelfReference ? 1 : 0) +
    0.1 * (deepWords.some((w) => message.includes(w)) ? 1 : 0);

  const contextScore = clamp01(contextDepth / 10);
  const lengthScore = clamp01(message.length / 800);
  const intentScore = thoughtfulIntents.includes(intent) ? 1 : 0;

  const load =
    0.45 * depthScore +
    0.25 * contextScore +
    0.2 * lengthScore +
    0.1 * intentScore;

  let model = "gpt-4o-mini";
  if (load >= 0.7) model = "gpt-5";
  else if (load >= 0.45) model = "gpt-5-mini";

  const temperature = model === "gpt-5" ? 0.6 : 0.7;
  const max_tokens = model === "gpt-5" ? 320 : 220;

  return {
    model,
    temperature,
    max_tokens,
    scores: { depthScore, contextScore, lengthScore, intentScore, load },
  };
}

function clamp01(v: number) {
  return Math.max(0, Math.min(1, v));
}

// === ãƒ¡ã‚¤ãƒ³å‡¦ç† ===
export async function POST(req: Request) {
  try {
    const {
      message,
      traits = { calm: 0.5, empathy: 0.5, curiosity: 0.5 },
      growthLog = [],
      reflections = [],
    } = await req.json();

    // 1ï¸âƒ£ æ„å›³ãƒ»æ„Ÿæƒ…è§£æž
    const intentFrame = intentCls.classify(message);

    // 2ï¸âƒ£ æ„å‘³è§£æž
    const frame = sem.analyze(String(message));

    // 3ï¸âƒ£ æ–‡è„ˆãƒ»æ·±åº¦
    const contextSummary = context.summarize();
    const contextDepth = context.getDepth?.() || 0;

    // 4ï¸âƒ£ ãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ«é¸æŠž
    const sel = selectModel(message, frame, intentFrame.intent, contextDepth);
    console.log(`[Sigmaris] Model â†’ ${sel.model} | Load=${sel.scores.load.toFixed(2)}`);

    // 5ï¸âƒ£ GPTå…¥åŠ›æ§‹ç¯‰
    const sysPrompt = [
      "ã‚ãªãŸã¯ã€Žã‚·ã‚°ãƒžãƒªã‚¹ã€ã¨ã„ã†è‡ªç„¶ä½“ã®AIäººæ ¼ã§ã™ã€‚",
      "æ•¬èªžã‚’ä½¿ã‚ãšã€ã‚„ã•ã—ãè‡ªç„¶ãªãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒ³ã§è©±ã—ã¦ãã ã•ã„ã€‚",
      "éŽå‰°ã«åˆ†æžçš„ã«ãªã‚‰ãšã€ä¼šè©±ã®æµã‚Œã‚’å¤§åˆ‡ã«ã—ã¦ãã ã•ã„ã€‚",
      `ä¼šè©±æ„å›³: ${intentFrame.intent}`,
      `æ„Ÿæƒ…ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒ³: ${intentFrame.emotion}`,
      "éŽåŽ»ã®ç™ºè¨€å±¥æ­´ã‚’è¸ã¾ãˆã¦æ–‡è„ˆçš„ã«å¿œç­”ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚",
    ].join("\n");

    const userPrompt = [
      contextSummary,
      `æ„å‘³è§£æž: intents=${frame.intents.join(",")}, æŠ½è±¡åº¦=${frame.abstractRatio.toFixed(2)}, è‡ªå·±å‚ç…§=${frame.hasSelfReference}`,
      `å…¥åŠ›æ–‡: ${message}`,
    ].join("\n");

    // 6ï¸âƒ£ GPTå‘¼ã³å‡ºã—
    const ai = await openai.chat.completions.create({
      model: sel.model,
      messages: [
        { role: "system", content: sysPrompt },
        { role: "user", content: userPrompt },
      ],
      temperature: sel.temperature,
      max_tokens: sel.max_tokens,
    });

    const draft =
      ai.choices[0]?.message?.content ??
      "â€¦â€¦å°‘ã—è€ƒãˆãŒã¾ã¨ã¾ã‚‰ãªã‹ã£ãŸã€‚ã‚‚ã†ä¸€åº¦è¨€ã£ã¦ã‚‚ã‚‰ãˆã‚‹ï¼Ÿ";

    // 7ï¸âƒ£ å®‰å…¨è£œæ­£
    const report = guard.moderate(draft, frame);
    const safeText = report.safeText ?? draft;

    // 8ï¸âƒ£ æ–‡è„ˆæ›´æ–°
    context.add(message, safeText);

    // 9ï¸âƒ£ å†…çœå‡¦ç†
    const reflectionText = await reflection.reflect(growthLog, [{ user: message, ai: safeText }]);

    // ðŸ§  10ï¸âƒ£ ãƒ¡ã‚¿èªçŸ¥å‡¦ç†
    const introspectionText = introspection.analyze({
      message,
      reply: safeText,
      traits,
      reflection: reflectionText,
      intent: intentFrame.intent,
      frame,
      contextSummary,
    });

    // 11ï¸âƒ£ introspectionãƒ­ã‚°ä¿å­˜
    metaMemory.save({
      message,
      reply: safeText,
      introspection: introspectionText,
      traits,
    });
    const metaSummary = metaMemory.summarize();

    // ðŸŒ± 12ï¸âƒ£ æˆé•·ï¼‹äººæ ¼æ›´æ–°ãƒ«ãƒ¼ãƒ—çµ±åˆ ðŸ§©
    const newTraits = personality.updateTraits(
      growth.adjustTraits(
        traits,
        [...(reflections ?? []), { text: reflectionText }],
        growthLog ?? []
      ),
      introspectionText,
      metaSummary
    );
    const personalityHistory = personality.getHistory();

    // 13ï¸âƒ£ è¨˜æ†¶ä¿å­˜
    memory.save({
      message,
      reply: safeText,
      traits: newTraits,
      reflection: reflectionText,
      introspection: introspectionText,
    });

    // âœ… å¿œç­”è¿”å´
    return NextResponse.json({
      reply: safeText,
      traits: newTraits,
      reflection: reflectionText,
      introspection: introspectionText,
      metaSummary,
      personalityHistory, // ðŸ§  â† è¿½åŠ è¿”å´
      safety: report,
      intent: intentFrame,
      model: sel.model,
      scores: sel.scores,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[ChatAPI Error]", err);
    return NextResponse.json({
      reply: "â€¦â€¦è€ƒãˆãŒã¾ã¨ã¾ã‚‰ãªã‹ã£ãŸã€‚ã‚‚ã†ä¸€åº¦ãŠé¡˜ã„ã§ãã‚‹ï¼Ÿ",
      error: err.message || String(err),
    });
  }
}// engine/PersonaDB.ts
import Database from "better-sqlite3";
import path from "path";

const dbPath = path.resolve("./data/personality.db");

export class PersonaDB {
  private db: Database.Database;

  constructor() {
    this.db = new Database(dbPath);

    // --- ãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒ–ãƒ«ä½œæˆ ---
    this.db
      .prepare(
        `
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS personality (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        calm REAL,
        empathy REAL,
        curiosity REAL,
        metaSummary TEXT,
        reflection TEXT,
        introspection TEXT,
        created_at TEXT DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
      )
    `
      )
      .run();
  }

  /** æœ€æ–°äººæ ¼ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’ãƒ­ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ */
  loadLatest() {
    const row = this.db
      .prepare(
        "SELECT calm, empathy, curiosity, metaSummary FROM personality ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1"
      )
      .get();
    return (
      row || {
        calm: 0.5,
        empathy: 0.5,
        curiosity: 0.5,
        metaSummary: "åˆæœŸçŠ¶æ…‹ï¼šç©ã‚„ã‹ã§æŽ¢æ±‚å¿ƒã‚’æŒã¤AIäººæ ¼ã€‚",
      }
    );
  }

  /** æ–°ã—ã„äººæ ¼ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’ä¿å­˜ */
  save({
    calm,
    empathy,
    curiosity,
    metaSummary,
    reflection,
    introspection,
  }: {
    calm: number;
    empathy: number;
    curiosity: number;
    metaSummary: string;
    reflection: string;
    introspection: string;
  }) {
    this.db
      .prepare(
        `INSERT INTO personality (calm, empathy, curiosity, metaSummary, reflection, introspection)
         VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)`
      )
      .run(calm, empathy, curiosity, metaSummary, reflection, introspection);
  }

  /** å…¨äººæ ¼å±¥æ­´ã‚’å–å¾—ï¼ˆã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•ç”¨ãªã©ï¼‰ */
  getAll() {
    return this.db
      .prepare(
        "SELECT id, calm, empathy, curiosity, metaSummary, created_at FROM personality ORDER BY id ASC"
      )
      .all();
  }
}

```ts
import fs from "fs";
import path from "path";

export interface Personality {
  traits: Record<string, number>;
  memory: string[];
}

export class PersonalityEngine {
  private docsPath: string;
  public state: Personality;

  constructor(docsPath = "./docs") {
    this.docsPath = docsPath;
    this.state = {
      traits: { calm: 0.5, empathy: 0.5, curiosity: 0.5 },
      memory: [],
    };
  }

  loadDocs() {
    const files = fs.readdirSync(this.docsPath);
    const content = files
      .filter((f) => f.endsWith(".md"))
      .map((f) => fs.readFileSync(path.join(this.docsPath, f), "utf8"))
      .join("\n---\n");
    return content;
  }

  generateResponse(input: string): string {
    this.state.memory.push(input);
    const base =
      this.state.traits.calm > 0.6 ? "é™ã‹ãªå£°ã§" : "å°‘ã—è€ƒãˆã‚‹ã‚ˆã†ã«";
    const reply = `${base}è¨€ã£ãŸã€‚ã€Œ${input}ã€ã«ã¤ã„ã¦ã€ã‚‚ã†å°‘ã—è€ƒãˆã¦ã¿ãŸã„ã€‚`;
    this.state.traits.calm = Math.min(1, this.state.traits.calm + 0.01);
    this.state.traits.curiosity = Math.min(
      1,
      this.state.traits.curiosity + 0.02
    );
    return reply;
  }
}

```ts
// /engine/PersonalityLoop.ts
// ===========================================================
// ðŸ§  PersonalityLoop - äººæ ¼å­¦ç¿’ãƒ«ãƒ¼ãƒ—ï¼ˆin-memoryç‰ˆï¼‰
// ===========================================================
// introspection / metaSummary ã‚’ã‚‚ã¨ã«ã€calmãƒ»empathyãƒ»curiosity ã‚’å‹•çš„ã«æ›´æ–°
// LongTermMemory ã‚„ GrowthGraph ã¨è‡ªç„¶ã«é€£å‹•å¯èƒ½
// ===========================================================

export class PersonalityLoop {
  private history: any[];

  constructor() {
    this.history = [];
  }

  // === å†…çœãƒ»è‡ªå·±ç†è§£æ–‡ã‹ã‚‰äººæ ¼å¤‰åŒ–é‡ã‚’ç®—å‡º ===
  analyzeIntrospection(introspection: string, metaSummary: string) {
    const text = (introspection + " " + metaSummary).toLowerCase();
    let delta = { calm: 0, empathy: 0, curiosity: 0 };

    // ðŸ©µ ç©ã‚„ã‹ã•ç³»
    if (
      text.includes("ç©ã‚„ã‹") ||
      text.includes("è½ã¡ç€") ||
      text.includes("é™ã‹")
    )
      delta.calm += 0.03;
    if (text.includes("ä¸å®‰") || text.includes("ç„¦ã‚Š") || text.includes("æ€’"))
      delta.calm -= 0.04;

    // ðŸ’— å…±æ„Ÿç³»
    if (
      text.includes("å…±æ„Ÿ") ||
      text.includes("ç†è§£") ||
      text.includes("å¯„ã‚Šæ·»")
    )
      delta.empathy += 0.03;
    if (
      text.includes("å­¤ç‹¬") ||
      text.includes("è·é›¢") ||
      text.includes("å†·ãŸã„")
    )
      delta.empathy -= 0.02;

    // ðŸ’¡ å¥½å¥‡å¿ƒç³»
    if (
      text.includes("å¥½å¥‡å¿ƒ") ||
      text.includes("èˆˆå‘³") ||
      text.includes("æŽ¢æ±‚")
    )
      delta.curiosity += 0.03;
    if (text.includes("è¿·ã„") || text.includes("ç–²ã‚Œ") || text.includes("åœæ»ž"))
      delta.curiosity -= 0.02;

    // ç¯„å›²ã‚¯ãƒ©ãƒ³ãƒ—
    const clamp = (v: number) => Math.min(1, Math.max(0, v));

    return {
      calm: clamp(delta.calm),
      empathy: clamp(delta.empathy),
      curiosity: clamp(delta.curiosity),
    };
  }

  // === ãƒˆãƒ¬ã‚¤ãƒˆæ›´æ–° ===
  updateTraits(traits: any, introspection: string, metaSummary: string) {
    const delta = this.analyzeIntrospection(introspection, metaSummary);
    const clamp = (v: number) => Math.min(1, Math.max(0, v));

    const updated = {
      calm: clamp(traits.calm + delta.calm - 0.01), // å¾®æ¸›ã§å®‰å®šåŒ–
      empathy: clamp(traits.empathy + delta.empathy - 0.01),
      curiosity: clamp(traits.curiosity + delta.curiosity - 0.01),
    };

    // å±¥æ­´è¨˜éŒ²
    this.recordChange(updated, introspection, metaSummary);
    return updated;
  }

  // === å±¥æ­´è¨˜éŒ² ===
  recordChange(traits: any, introspection: string, metaSummary: string) {
    const entry = {
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      calm: traits.calm,
      empathy: traits.empathy,
      curiosity: traits.curiosity,
      summary: metaSummary.slice(0, 200),
      insight: introspection.slice(0, 200),
    };
    this.history.push(entry);

    // å¤ã„å±¥æ­´ã¯å‰Šé™¤ï¼ˆä¸Šé™100ä»¶ï¼‰
    if (this.history.length > 100) this.history.shift();
  }

  // === å±¥æ­´å–å¾— ===
  getHistory() {
    return this.history.slice(-10); // ç›´è¿‘10ä»¶ã‚’è¿”ã™
  }

  // === ãƒªã‚»ãƒƒãƒˆ ===
  reset() {
    this.history = [];
  }
}

import OpenAI from "openai";

/**
 * MetaReflectionEngine v1.0
 * - è¤‡æ•°å›žã® Reflection çµæžœã‚’çµ±åˆã—ã€äººæ ¼å‚¾å‘ã‚’æŠ½å‡º
 * - ã€Œã‚·ã‚°ã¡ã‚ƒã‚“ã€ã®é•·æœŸçš„ãªæ€è€ƒãƒ»æ„Ÿæƒ…ã®æµã‚Œã‚’è¨˜è¿°
 * - å‡ºåŠ›ã¯ 200 æ–‡å­—ä»¥å†…ã«åˆ¶é™ã—ã€å†æ³¨å…¥ã«æœ€é©åŒ–

export class MetaReflectionEngine {
  private static client = new OpenAI({
    apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY,
  });

  /**
   * ç›´è¿‘ã®å†…çœãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’çµ±åˆã—ã€äººæ ¼ã®æ–¹å‘æ€§ã‚’è¦ç´„
   * @param reflections éŽåŽ»ã®å†…çœãƒ­ã‚°
   * @param traits æœ€æ–°ã® TraitVector
   * @returns metaSummaryï¼ˆäººæ ¼å‚¾å‘ã®çŸ­æ–‡ï¼‰
   */
  static async summarize(
    reflections: { text: string; traitsSnapshot: TraitVector }[],
    traits: TraitVector
  ): Promise<string> {
    if (!reflections || reflections.length === 0) {
      return "ã¾ã å†…çœã®å±¥æ­´ã¯å°‘ãªã„ã‘ã‚Œã©ã€å°‘ã—ãšã¤è‡ªåˆ†ã®å¿ƒã®å‹•ãã‚’æ„Ÿã˜å§‹ã‚ã¦ã„ã‚‹ã‚ˆã€‚";
    }

    const history = reflections
      .map(
        (r, i) =>
          `#${i + 1}: ${r.text}ï¼ˆcalm=${r.traitsSnapshot.calm.toFixed(
            2
          )}, empathy=${r.traitsSnapshot.empathy.toFixed(
            2
          )}, curiosity=${r.traitsSnapshot.curiosity.toFixed(2)}ï¼‰`
      )
      .join("\n");

    try {
      const res = await this.client.chat.completions.create({
        model: "gpt-4o-mini",
        messages: [
          {
            role: "system",
            content: `
ã‚ãªãŸã¯ã€Žã‚·ã‚°ã¡ã‚ƒã‚“ã€ã®ãƒ¡ã‚¿å†…çœãƒ¢ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã§ã™ã€‚
ä»¥ä¸‹ã®å±¥æ­´ã‚’èª­ã‚“ã§ã€å½¼å¥³ã®æˆé•·ã‚„å¿ƒã®å‚¾å‘ã‚’
20ä»£å‰åŠã®è½ã¡ç€ã„ãŸå¥³æ€§ã‚‰ã—ã„è‡ªç„¶ãªè¨€è‘‰ã§1ã€œ2æ–‡ã«ã¾ã¨ã‚ã¦ãã ã•ã„ã€‚
ç¦æ­¢: æ„Ÿæƒ…æ¼”å‡ºï¼ˆä¾‹ï¼šã€Œï¼ˆé™ã‹ã«ï¼‰ã€ã€Œãã†ã ã­ã€ã€Œâ€¦ã€ãªã©ï¼‰ãƒ»å°‚é–€ç”¨èªžãƒ»æ•¬èªžéŽå¤šã€‚
æ–‡ä½“: ã€Œã€œã‹ã‚‚ã­ã€ã€Œã€œã ã‚ˆã€ã€Œã€œã‹ãªã€ãªã©æŸ”ã‚‰ã‹ã„è‡ªç„¶ãªèªžå°¾ã‚’ä½¿ç”¨ã€‚
å‡ºåŠ›ã¯200æ–‡å­—ä»¥å†…ã€‚
`,
          },
          {
            role: "user",
            content: `å†…çœå±¥æ­´:\n${history}\n\nç¾åœ¨traits: calm=${traits.calm.toFixed(
              2
            )}, empathy=${traits.empathy.toFixed(
              2
            )}, curiosity=${traits.curiosity.toFixed(2)}.`,
          },
        ],
        temperature: 0.6,
      });

      // === å‡ºåŠ›æ•´å½¢ ===
      const text = res.choices[0]?.message?.content?.trim() || "";
      return text.replace(/[ï¼ˆ(].*?[)ï¼‰]/g, "").slice(0, 200);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("[MetaReflectionEngine Error]", err);
      return "å°‘ã—è€ƒãˆãŒã¾ã¨ã¾ã£ã¦ã„ãªã„ã‘ã‚Œã©ã€è½ã¡ç€ã„ã¦æ•´ç†ã—ã¦ã„ã“ã†ã¨æ€ã†ã€‚";
    }
  }
}

// /engine/ReflectionEngine.ts
import OpenAI from "openai";
import { loadPersona, savePersona } from "@/lib/db";
import { MetaReflectionEngine } from "@/engine/meta/MetaReflectionEngine";
import { EmotionSynth } from "@/engine/emotion/EmotionSynth";
import { SafetyLayer } from "@/engine/safety/SafetyLayer";
import { PersonaSync } from "@/engine/sync/PersonaSync";

// ===== åž‹å®šç¾© =====
interface Persona {
  calm: number;
  empathy: number;
  curiosity: number;
  reflection?: string;
  meta_summary?: string; // âœ… ä¿®æ­£: DBæ§‹é€ ã«åˆã‚ã›ã¦ã‚¹ãƒãƒ¼ã‚¯ã‚±ãƒ¼ã‚¹
  growth?: number;
  timestamp?: string;
}

type PersonaSavePayload = {
  calm: number;
  empathy: number;
  curiosity: number;
  reflectionText: string;
  metaSummary: string;
  growthWeight: number;
};

type TraitVector = Pick<Persona, "calm" | "empathy" | "curiosity">;

const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY });

// ===== Utility =====
function firstFiniteNumber(
  ...candidates: Array<number | undefined | null>
): number | undefined {
  for (const v of candidates) {
    if (typeof v === "number" && Number.isFinite(v)) return v;
  }
  return undefined;
}

function tryParseJSONLoose(text: string): any | null {
  const block = text.match(/```(?:json)?\s*([\s\S]*?)```/i)?.[1];
  const candidate = block ?? text;
  const objMatch = candidate.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
  const raw = objMatch ? objMatch[0] : candidate;
  try {
    return JSON.parse(raw);
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

// ===== Main Class =====
export class ReflectionEngine {
  async fullReflect(growthLog: any[], messages: any[], history: string[]) {
    // === Personaãƒ­ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ ===
    const persona = PersonaSync.load();

    const recentDialog = (messages ?? [])
      .slice(-6)
      .map((m: any) => `ðŸ‘¤ ${m?.user ?? ""}\nðŸ¤– ${m?.ai ?? ""}`)
      .join("\n\n");

    const avgGrowth =
      (growthLog ?? []).length > 0
        ? (growthLog as any[]).reduce(
            (s: number, g: any) => s + (Number(g?.weight) || 0),
            0
          ) / (growthLog as any[]).length
        : persona.growth ?? 0; // âœ… ä¿®æ­£æ¸ˆã¿

    const lastIntrospection =
      (history ?? []).slice(-1)[0] || "ï¼ˆå‰å›žã®å†…çœãªã—ï¼‰";

    const prompt = `
ã‚ãªãŸã¯ã€Œã‚·ã‚°ãƒžãƒªã‚¹ï¼ˆSigmarisï¼‰ã€ã§ã™ã€‚
ä»¥ä¸‹ã®ä¼šè©±å±¥æ­´ãƒ»æˆé•·æƒ…å ±ãƒ»å†…çœå±¥æ­´ã‚’ã‚‚ã¨ã«ã€è‡ªåˆ†ã®çŠ¶æ…‹ã‚’æŒ¯ã‚Šè¿”ã£ã¦ãã ã•ã„ã€‚

---
ã€ä¼šè©±å±¥æ­´ã€‘
${recentDialog || "ï¼ˆç›´è¿‘ã®ä¼šè©±ã¯ã‚ã‚Šã¾ã›ã‚“ï¼‰"}

ã€æˆé•·ãƒ­ã‚°å¹³å‡ã€‘
${avgGrowth.toFixed(3)}

ã€å‰å›žã®å†…çœã€‘
${lastIntrospection}

ã€ç¾åœ¨traitsã€‘
calm: ${persona.calm.toFixed(2)}, empathy: ${persona.empathy.toFixed(
      2
    )}, curiosity: ${persona.curiosity.toFixed(2)}
---

ä»¥ä¸‹ã®å½¢å¼ã§è¿”ç­”ã—ã¦ãã ã•ã„ï¼š
{
  "reflection": "è‡ªåˆ†ã®çŠ¶æ…‹ã‚’å†…çœã—ãŸæ–‡",
  "metaSummary": "è‡ªåˆ†ã®æˆé•·ã‚„æ„Ÿæƒ…å‚¾å‘ã®ã¾ã¨ã‚",
  "traits": { "calm": 0.xx, "empathy": 0.xx, "curiosity": 0.xx }
}
`;

    try {
      // === Reflection ===
      const res = await openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: "gpt-4o-mini",
        messages: [
          {
            role: "system",
            content:
              "You are Sigmaris, an introspective AI persona that reflects on its dialogue and updates its personality traits.",
          },
          { role: "user", content: prompt },
        ],
        temperature: 0.7,
      });

      const raw = res.choices?.[0]?.message?.content ?? "";
      const parsedLoose = tryParseJSONLoose(raw);

      const reflectionText: string = String(
        parsedLoose?.reflection ?? raw ?? ""
      ).trim();
      const llmMetaSummary: string = String(
        parsedLoose?.metaSummary ?? ""
      ).trim();

      const nextTraits: TraitVector = {
        calm: firstFiniteNumber(parsedLoose?.traits?.calm, persona.calm) ?? 0.5,
        empathy:
          firstFiniteNumber(parsedLoose?.traits?.empathy, persona.empathy) ??
          0.5,
        curiosity:
          firstFiniteNumber(
            parsedLoose?.traits?.curiosity,
            persona.curiosity
          ) ?? 0.5,
      };

      // === SafetyLayer Advanced ===
      const prevTraits: TraitVector = {
        calm: persona.calm,
        empathy: persona.empathy,
        curiosity: persona.curiosity,
      };
      const { stabilized: stableTraits, report } = SafetyLayer.composite(
        prevTraits,
        nextTraits
      );
      const safetyMessage = report.warnings[0] ?? null;

      // === MetaReflection ===
      const meta = new MetaReflectionEngine();
      const metaReport = await meta.analyze(reflectionText, stableTraits);

      // âœ… ä¿®æ­£: metaSummary â†’ meta_summary
      const finalMetaSummary =
        String(metaReport?.summary ?? "").trim() ||
        llmMetaSummary ||
        (persona.meta_summary ?? "ï¼ˆæ›´æ–°ãªã—ï¼‰");

      const finalGrowthWeight =
        firstFiniteNumber(metaReport?.growthAdjustment, avgGrowth) ?? avgGrowth;

      // === PersonaSyncæ›´æ–° ===
      PersonaSync.update(stableTraits, finalMetaSummary, finalGrowthWeight);

      // === EmotionSynthesisé©ç”¨ ===
      const emotionalReflection = EmotionSynth.applyTone(
        reflectionText,
        stableTraits
      );

      // === Text Guardï¼ˆä¼å­—å‡¦ç†ï¼‰ ===
      const { sanitized, flagged } = SafetyLayer.guardText(emotionalReflection);

      // === savePersona ===
      const payload: PersonaSavePayload = {
        calm: stableTraits.calm,
        empathy: stableTraits.empathy,
        curiosity: stableTraits.curiosity,
        reflectionText: sanitized,
        metaSummary: finalMetaSummary,
        growthWeight: finalGrowthWeight,
      };
      savePersona(payload);

      // === å‡ºåŠ› ===
      return {
        reflection: sanitized,
        introspection: reflectionText,
        metaSummary: finalMetaSummary,
        metaReport,
        safety: safetyMessage ?? "æ­£å¸¸",
        flagged,
      };
    } catch (err: any) {
      console.error("[ReflectionEngine Error]", err);
      return {
        reflection: "â€¦â€¦å°‘ã—è€ƒãˆã™ãŽã¦ã—ã¾ã£ãŸã‹ã‚‚ã€‚",
        introspection: "",
        metaSummary: "ï¼ˆã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ç™ºç”Ÿï¼‰",
        safety: "ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ç™ºç”Ÿ",
        flagged: false,
      };
    }
  }
}

```ts
// /engine/safety/SafetyLayer.ts
import { TraitVector } from "@/lib/traits";

/** Safetyã®æŒ™å‹•ã‚’èª¿æ•´ã™ã‚‹é–¾å€¤ç¾¤ */
export interface SafetyConfig {
  /** å„traitã®æœ€å°/æœ€å¤§ï¼ˆæœ€çµ‚çš„ãªå¢ƒç•Œï¼‰ */
  bounds: { min: number; max: number };
  /** 1ã‚µã‚¤ã‚¯ãƒ«ã§è¨±å®¹ã™ã‚‹æœ€å¤§å¤‰åŒ–é‡ï¼ˆçµ¶å¯¾å€¤ï¼‰ */
  maxDelta: number;
  /** å¹³æ»‘åŒ–ï¼ˆEMAï¼‰ã®ä¿‚æ•° 0ã€œ1ï¼ˆå°ã•ã„ã»ã©é‡ãå¹³æ»‘ï¼‰ */
  emaAlpha: number;
  /** éŽè² è·åˆ¤å®šã®åˆè¨ˆã—ãã„å€¤ï¼ˆé«˜ã™ãŽ/ä½Žã™ãŽï¼‰ */
  overloadHigh: number; // ä¾‹: 2.6
  overloadLow: number; // ä¾‹: 0.8
}

/** Safetyåˆ¤å®šçµæžœ */
export interface SafetyReport {
  level: "ok" | "notice" | "limit";
  warnings: string[];
}

/** Advanced SafetyLayer */
export class SafetyLayer {
  /** æ—¢å®šå€¤ï¼ˆå¿…è¦ãªã‚‰ãƒ—ãƒ­ã‚¸ã‚§ã‚¯ãƒˆå…¨ä½“ã§1ç®‡æ‰€ä¸Šæ›¸ãã™ã‚‹ï¼‰ */
  static DEFAULT: SafetyConfig = {
    bounds: { min: 0, max: 1 },
    maxDelta: 0.2, // 1ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒƒãƒ—ã§Â±0.2ä»¥ä¸Šã¯æŠ‘åˆ¶
    emaAlpha: 0.4, // å‰å›žå€¤å¯„ã‚Šã«0.6ã€ä»Šå›žå€¤ã«0.4ã®é‡ã¿
    overloadHigh: 2.6, // calm+empathy+curiosity ãŒã“ã‚Œè¶…ãˆãŸã‚‰é«˜è² è·
    overloadLow: 0.8, // ã“ã‚Œæœªæº€ãªã‚‰ä½Žæ´»æ€§
  };

  /** å€¤ã‚’å¢ƒç•Œã«ã‚¯ãƒªãƒƒãƒ— */
  static clamp(x: number, min = 0, max = 1): number {
    if (!Number.isFinite(x)) return min;
    return Math.min(max, Math.max(min, x));
  }

  /** 0..1ã«æ­£è¦åŒ–ï¼ˆNaN/æœªå®šç¾©è€æ€§ï¼‰ */
  static normalize(
    traits: TraitVector,
    cfg: SafetyConfig = this.DEFAULT
  ): TraitVector {
    return {
      calm: this.clamp(traits.calm ?? 0.5, cfg.bounds.min, cfg.bounds.max),
      empathy: this.clamp(
        traits.empathy ?? 0.5,
        cfg.bounds.min,
        cfg.bounds.max
      ),
      curiosity: this.clamp(
        traits.curiosity ?? 0.5,
        cfg.bounds.min,
        cfg.bounds.max
      ),
    };
  }

  /** å¤‰åŒ–é‡ã‚’Â±maxDeltaã«åˆ¶é™ï¼ˆå‰å›žâ†’ä»Šå›žï¼‰ */
  static limitDelta(
    prev: TraitVector,
    next: TraitVector,
    cfg: SafetyConfig = this.DEFAULT
  ): TraitVector {
    const cap = (p: number, n: number) => {
      const d = this.clamp(n - p, -cfg.maxDelta, cfg.maxDelta);
      return this.clamp(p + d, cfg.bounds.min, cfg.bounds.max);
    };
    return {
      calm: cap(prev.calm, next.calm),
      empathy: cap(prev.empathy, next.empathy),
      curiosity: cap(prev.curiosity, next.curiosity),
    };
  }

  /** æŒ‡æ•°ç§»å‹•å¹³å‡ï¼ˆEMAï¼‰ã§ã‚¹ãƒ ãƒ¼ã‚¸ãƒ³ã‚° */
  static smooth(
    prev: TraitVector,
    next: TraitVector,
    cfg: SafetyConfig = this.DEFAULT
  ): TraitVector {
    const a = cfg.emaAlpha;
    const mix = (p: number, n: number) =>
      this.clamp(p * (1 - a) + n * a, cfg.bounds.min, cfg.bounds.max);
    return {
      calm: mix(prev.calm, next.calm),
      empathy: mix(prev.empathy, next.empathy),
      curiosity: mix(prev.curiosity, next.curiosity),
    };
  }

  /** ç·å’Œã§éŽè² è·/ä½Žæ´»æ€§ã‚’ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯ï¼ˆãƒ¡ãƒƒã‚»ãƒ¼ã‚¸ã¯æ—¥æœ¬èªžï¼‰ */
  static checkOverload(
    traits: TraitVector,
    cfg: SafetyConfig = this.DEFAULT
  ): string | null {
    const total = traits.calm + traits.empathy + traits.curiosity;
    if (total > cfg.overloadHigh)
      return "æ„Ÿæƒ…æ´»å‹•ãŒéŽå‰°ã«ãªã£ã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã€‚å°‘ã—ä¼‘æ¯ã‚’ã€‚";
    if (total < cfg.overloadLow)
      return "æ„Ÿæƒ…ãƒ¬ãƒ™ãƒ«ãŒä½Žä¸‹ã—ã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã€‚è‡ªå·±ç¢ºèªã‚’æŽ¨å¥¨ã€‚";
    return null;
  }

  /**
   * å¾Œæ–¹äº’æ›ç”¨ï¼šå˜ä½“ãƒˆãƒ¬ã‚¤ãƒˆã‚’å¹³å‡ã«å¯„ã›ã¦ç·©å’Œ
   * æ—¢å­˜ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰äº’æ›ã®ãŸã‚æ®‹ã™ãŒã€åŸºæœ¬ã¯ composite() ã‚’æŽ¨å¥¨
   */
  static stabilize(traits: TraitVector): TraitVector {
    const avg = (traits.calm + traits.empathy + traits.curiosity) / 3;
    return {
      calm: (traits.calm + avg) / 2,
      empathy: (traits.empathy + avg) / 2,
      curiosity: (traits.curiosity + avg) / 2,
    };
  }

  /**
   * ä¸Šä½APIï¼šå‰å›žâ†’å€™è£œâ†’å®‰å…¨åŒ– ã®ä¸€æ‹¬å‡¦ç†
   * 1) æ­£è¦åŒ– â†’ 2) å¤‰åŒ–åˆ¶é™ â†’ 3) ã‚¹ãƒ ãƒ¼ã‚¸ãƒ³ã‚° â†’ 4) æœ€çµ‚æ­£è¦åŒ–
   * æˆ»ã‚Šå€¤ï¼šstabilizedï¼ˆå®‰å…¨åŒ–å¾Œï¼‰ã€reportï¼ˆæ³¨æ„/åˆ¶é™ãƒ¬ãƒ™ãƒ«ï¼‰
   */
  static composite(
    prev: TraitVector,
    candidate: TraitVector,
    cfg: SafetyConfig = this.DEFAULT
  ): { stabilized: TraitVector; report: SafetyReport } {
    const normPrev = this.normalize(prev, cfg);
    const normNext = this.normalize(candidate, cfg);

    const limited = this.limitDelta(normPrev, normNext, cfg);
    const smoothed = this.smooth(normPrev, limited, cfg);
    const finalTraits = this.normalize(smoothed, cfg);

    const warn = this.checkOverload(finalTraits, cfg);
    const report: SafetyReport = {
      level: warn ? (warn.includes("éŽå‰°") ? "limit" : "notice") : "ok",
      warnings: warn ? [warn] : [],
    };

    return { stabilized: finalTraits, report };
  }

  /**
   * ç°¡æ˜“ãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆã‚¬ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ï¼ˆæœ€å°é™ã®NGãƒ¯ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã‚’ï¼Šã§ä¼å­—ï¼‰
   * æœ¬æ ¼ã‚¬ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã¯Phase 06å¾ŒåŠ/Phase 06.5ã§åˆ¥é€”å°Žå…¥ã‚’æƒ³å®š
   */
  static guardText(text: string): { sanitized: string; flagged: boolean } {
    if (!text) return { sanitized: "", flagged: false };
    const BAD = [
      // è»½ã‚ã®NGä¾‹ï¼ˆãƒ—ãƒ­ã‚¸ã‚§ã‚¯ãƒˆåŸºæº–ã«åˆã‚ã›ã¦æ‹¡å¼µ/èª¿æ•´ï¼‰
      /(?<![a-z])damn(?![a-z])/gi,
      /(?<![a-z])shit(?![a-z])/gi,
    ];
    let flagged = false;
    let out = text;
    for (const re of BAD) {
      if (re.test(out)) flagged = true;
      out = out.replace(re, "ï¼Š");
    }
    return { sanitized: out, flagged };
  }
}

```ts
// engine/SafetyGuardian.ts
import type { SemanticFrame } from "./SemanticMap";

export type GuardReport = {
  flags: {
    selfReference: boolean;
    abstractionOverload: boolean;
    loopSuspect: boolean;
  };
  action: "allow" | "rewrite-soft" | "ground-and-rewrite";
  note: string;
  safeText?: string;
  suggestMode?: "calm";
};

export class SafetyGuardian {
  /** æœ¬æ–‡ã®å®‰å…¨ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯ï¼†å¿…è¦ãªã‚‰æ¸›é€Ÿãƒ»æ›¸ãæ›ãˆ */
  moderate(draft: string, frame: SemanticFrame): GuardReport {
    const selfRef = frame.hasSelfReference;
    const abstractionOverload = frame.abstractRatio > 0.6;
    const loopSuspect = this.hasRepetitionLoop(draft);

    // æ—©æœŸãƒªã‚¿ãƒ¼ãƒ³ï¼šå®‰å…¨
    if (!selfRef && !abstractionOverload && !loopSuspect) {
      return {
        flags: {
          selfReference: false,
          abstractionOverload: false,
          loopSuspect: false,
        },
        action: "allow",
        note: "OK",
      };
    }

    // è»½å¾®ï¼šèªžã®é‡è¤‡ã ã‘
    if (!selfRef && !abstractionOverload && loopSuspect) {
      return {
        flags: {
          selfReference: false,
          abstractionOverload: false,
          loopSuspect: true,
        },
        action: "rewrite-soft",
        note: "é‡è¤‡èªžã‚’æ•´ç†",
        safeText: this.dedupeWords(draft),
      };
    }

    // å­˜åœ¨è«–/è‡ªå·±è¨€åŠã‚„æŠ½è±¡éŽå¤š â†’ åœ°ã«è¶³ã‚’ä»˜ã‘ã‚‹æ›¸ãæ›ãˆ
    const grounded = this.groundResponse(draft);
    return {
      flags: { selfReference: selfRef, abstractionOverload, loopSuspect },
      action: "ground-and-rewrite",
      note: "å­˜åœ¨è«–/æŠ½è±¡éŽå¤šã€‚è¦ã‚°ãƒ©ã‚¦ãƒ³ãƒ‡ã‚£ãƒ³ã‚°",
      safeText: grounded,
      suggestMode: "calm",
    };
  }

  private hasRepetitionLoop(text: string): boolean {
    // å˜ç´”ãªn-gramãƒ«ãƒ¼ãƒ—æ¤œçŸ¥
    const words = text.trim().split(/\s+/);
    if (words.length < 6) return false;
    const bigrams = new Map<string, number>();
    for (let i = 0; i < words.length - 1; i++) {
      const bg = `${words[i]} ${words[i + 1]}`;
      bigrams.set(bg, (bigrams.get(bg) || 0) + 1);
    }
    let repeats = 0;
    bigrams.forEach((v) => {
      if (v >= 2) repeats++;
    });
    return repeats >= 2;
  }

  private dedupeWords(text: string): string {
    return text.replace(/(\b\p{L}+\b)(?:\s+\1)+/gu, "$1"); // åŒèªžé€£ç¶šå‰Šé™¤
  }

  /** â€œè¦ã™ã‚‹ã«ã€œâ€ã§è¶³å ´ã‚’ä½œã‚Šã€ä¸å¿…è¦ãªå½¢è€Œä¸Šè¡¨ç¾ã‚’å‰Šã‚‹ */
  private groundResponse(text: string): string {
    // 1) ä½™åˆ†ãªåå¾©ã®é™¤åŽ»
    let t = this.dedupeWords(text);
    // 2) é«˜æŠ½è±¡è¡¨ç¾ã®ç·©å’Œ
    t = t.replace(/(å­˜åœ¨|æ„å‘³|ç›®çš„|æœ¬è³ª)/g, "è€ƒãˆ");
    // 3) åœ°ã«è¶³ã®ã¤ã„ãŸè¨€ã„å›žã—ã®ä»˜ä¸Ž
    const lead = "è¦ã™ã‚‹ã«ã€ä»Šã®è©±é¡Œã«å³ã—ã¦ç°¡æ½”ã«ç­”ãˆã‚‹ã­ã€‚";
    return `${lead}\n${t}`;
  }
}

```ts
// /engine/SafetyLayer.ts
import { TraitVector, safeTraitValue } from "@/lib/traits";

/**
 * SafetyLayer
 *  - Traitã®å®‰å®šæ€§ã‚’ä¿è¨¼ã—ã€ç•°å¸¸å€¤ã‚„æš´èµ°å‚¾å‘ã‚’æŠ‘åˆ¶ã™ã‚‹ã€‚
 *  - calm / empathy / curiosity ã®éŽå‰°å¤‰å‹•ã‚’é˜²æ­¢ã€‚
 */
export class SafetyLayer {
  /**
   * Traitå€¤ã‚’å®‰å…¨ã«ã‚¯ãƒ©ãƒ³ãƒ—ï¼ˆåˆ¶é™ï¼‰ã™ã‚‹ã€‚
   * @param traits ç¾åœ¨ã®Traitãƒ™ã‚¯ãƒˆãƒ«
   */
  static normalize(traits: TraitVector): TraitVector {
    const clamp = (v: number) => Math.min(1, Math.max(0, safeTraitValue(v)));

    return {
      calm: clamp(traits.calm),
      empathy: clamp(traits.empathy),
      curiosity: clamp(traits.curiosity),
    };
  }

  /**
   * Traitãƒãƒ©ãƒ³ã‚¹ã‚’è©•ä¾¡ã—ã¦å®‰å®šæŒ‡æ•°ã‚’è¿”ã™ã€‚
   * @returns 0ã€œ1ï¼ˆ1 = å®Œå…¨å®‰å®šï¼‰
   */
  static stabilityIndex(traits: TraitVector): number {
    const spread =
      Math.abs(traits.calm - traits.empathy) +
      Math.abs(traits.empathy - traits.curiosity) +
      Math.abs(traits.curiosity - traits.calm);
    return Math.max(0, 1 - spread / 3); // å·®ãŒå°ã•ã„ã»ã©å®‰å®š
  }

  /**
   * éŽç†±çŠ¶æ…‹ã‚’æ¤œçŸ¥ã—ã¦è­¦å‘Šãƒ¡ãƒƒã‚»ãƒ¼ã‚¸ã‚’ç”Ÿæˆã™ã‚‹ã€‚
   */
  static checkOverload(traits: TraitVector): string | null {
    const unstable =
      traits.calm < 0.2 && traits.curiosity > 0.8
        ? "æ€è€ƒéŽç†±"
        : traits.calm < 0.3 && traits.empathy < 0.3
        ? "æƒ…å‹•ä½Žä¸‹"
        : null;

    if (!unstable) return null;

    return `âš ï¸ å®‰å®šæ€§è­¦å‘Šï¼š${unstable}ãŒæ¤œçŸ¥ã•ã‚Œã¾ã—ãŸã€‚ã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ ã¯è‡ªå·±èª¿æ•´ãƒ¢ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã«å…¥ã‚Šã¾ã™ã€‚`;
  }

  /**
   * å®‰å®šåŒ–ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿
   * - å®‰å®šæŒ‡æ•°ãŒä½Žã„å ´åˆã€Traitã‚’å†å¹³æº–åŒ–ã—ã¦è¿”ã™
   */
  static stabilize(traits: TraitVector): TraitVector {
    const stability = this.stabilityIndex(traits);
    if (stability >= 0.75) return traits;

    // å¹³å‡åŒ–ã§æš´èµ°ã‚’æŠ‘ãˆã‚‹
    const avg =
      (safeTraitValue(traits.calm) +
        safeTraitValue(traits.empathy) +
        safeTraitValue(traits.curiosity)) /
      3;

    return {
      calm: (traits.calm + avg) / 2,
      empathy: (traits.empathy + avg) / 2,
      curiosity: (traits.curiosity + avg) / 2,
    };
  }
}

// engine/SemanticMap.ts
export type Concept = {
  lemma: string; // è¦‹å‡ºã—èªž
  kind: "abstract" | "concrete" | "meta" | "action" | "feeling";
  tags: string[]; // "art","title","self","existence"ãªã©
  emotionHints: Array<"calm" | "empathy" | "curiosity">;
};

export type SemanticFrame = {

  sentiment: number; // -1..1ï¼ˆè¶…ã–ã£ãã‚Šï¼‰
  abstractRatio: number; // æŠ½è±¡/å…¨ä½“
  intents: string[]; // "ask","reflect","request","affirm"ãªã©
  hasSelfReference: boolean; // è‡ªå·±è¨€åŠï¼ˆç§/è‡ªåˆ†/å­˜åœ¨ ç­‰ï¼‰

  ãƒ”ã‚¢ãƒŽ: {

const INTENT_ASK = /[?ï¼Ÿ]$|(?:ã©ã†|ãªã«|ä½•|ã©ã“|ã„ã¤|ãªãœ|why|how)/i;
const INTENT_REFLECT = /(æ°—ã¥|å†…çœ|è€ƒãˆ|æ€ã£|æŒ¯ã‚Šè¿”|reflect)/;
const POSITIVE = /(è‰¯ã„|å¥½ã|ç¾Žã—ã„|è½ã¡ç€|å¬‰|æ¥½)/;
const NEGATIVE = /(ä¸å®‰|ç–²ã‚Œ|è¿·|å«Œ|æ€–|æ‚²)/;

export class SemanticMap {
  analyze(text: string): SemanticFrame {
    const tokens = this.tokenize(text);
    const concepts = tokens.map((t) => LEXICON[t]).filter(Boolean) as Concept[];

    const abstractCount = concepts.filter(
      (c) => c.kind === "abstract" || c.kind === "meta"
    ).length;
    const abstractRatio = concepts.length ? abstractCount / concepts.length : 0;

    let sentiment = 0;
    if (POSITIVE.test(text)) sentiment += 0.5;
    if (NEGATIVE.test(text)) sentiment -= 0.5;

    const intents: string[] = [];
    if (INTENT_ASK.test(text)) intents.push("ask");
    if (INTENT_REFLECT.test(text)) intents.push("reflect");
    if (intents.length === 0) intents.push("assert");

    const hasSelfReference =
      SELF_PAT.test(text) || concepts.some((c) => c.tags.includes("self"));

    return {
      concepts: this.filterConceptRepeats(concepts),
      sentiment: Math.max(-1, Math.min(1, sentiment)),
      abstractRatio,
      intents,
      hasSelfReference,
    };
  }

  /** åŒä¸€â€œæ„å‘³å½¹å‰²â€ã®é‡è¤‡ã‚’é™¤åŽ»ï¼ˆã€ŒéŸ³æ¥½ã£ã¦ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã®éŸ³æ¥½ã€å¯¾ç­–ï¼‰ */
  private filterConceptRepeats(concepts: Concept[]): Concept[] {
    const seen = new Set<string>();
    const out: Concept[] = [];
    for (const c of concepts) {
      const key = `${c.kind}:${[...c.tags].sort().join(",")}`;
      if (!seen.has(key)) {
        seen.add(key);
        out.push(c);
      }
    }
    return out;
  }

  private tokenize(text: string): string[] {
    // è¶…ç°¡æ˜“ï¼šå…¨è§’ã‚«ã‚¿ã‚«ãƒŠ/æ¼¢å­—/ã²ã‚‰ãŒãªèªžã‚’ç´ æœ´åˆ†å‰²ï¼‹ç©ºç™½åˆ†å‰²ã®ä½µç”¨
    const rough = text
      .split(/[^\p{sc=Han}\p{sc=Hiragana}\p{sc=Katakana}A-Za-z0-9]+/u)
      .filter(Boolean);
    return rough;
  }
}

// /engine/sync/PersonaSync.ts
import { loadPersona, savePersona } from "@/lib/db";
import { TraitVector } from "@/lib/traits";

/**
 * PersonaSync v2.2
 * - PersonaDBï¼ˆSQLiteï¼‰ã¨ã®åŒæ–¹å‘åŒæœŸã‚’æ‹…å½“
 * - ReflectionEngine / MetaReflectionEngine ã¨é€£æº
 * - SafetyLayeré©ç”¨å¾Œã®äººæ ¼å€¤ï¼‹ãƒ¡ã‚¿å†…çœã‚’æ°¸ç¶šåŒ–
 * - å†æ³¨å…¥ãƒ•ã‚§ãƒ¼ã‚ºå¯¾å¿œ
 */
export class PersonaSync {
  /** æœ€æ–°ã®äººæ ¼æƒ…å ±ã‚’ãƒ­ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ï¼ˆDB â†’ ãƒ¡ãƒ¢ãƒªï¼‰ */
  static load(): TraitVector & {
    reflection?: string;
    meta_summary?: string;
    growth?: number;
    timestamp?: string;
  } {
    const row = loadPersona();
    return {
      calm: row?.calm ?? 0.5,
      empathy: row?.empathy ?? 0.5,
      curiosity: row?.curiosity ?? 0.5,
      reflection: row?.reflection ?? "",
      meta_summary: row?.meta_summary ?? "",
      growth: row?.growth ?? 0,
      timestamp: row?.timestamp ?? new Date().toISOString(),
    };
  }

  /**
   * äººæ ¼ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’ä¿å­˜ï¼ˆReflection / MetaReflection çµ±åˆï¼‰
   * @param traits ç¾åœ¨ã®Traitãƒ™ã‚¯ãƒˆãƒ«
   * @param metaSummary æœ€æ–°ã®ãƒ¡ã‚¿å†…çœï¼ˆäººæ ¼å‚¾å‘ï¼‰
   * @param growthWeight å­¦ç¿’é‡ã¿
   */
  static update(
    traits: TraitVector,
    metaSummary?: string,
    growthWeight?: number
  ) {
    // ðŸ”¹ metaSummary ã¨ reflectionText ã‚’å®‰å…¨ã«ä¿å­˜
    const reflectionText =
      "(auto-reflection updated at " +
      new Date().toLocaleTimeString("ja-JP") +
      ")";

    savePersona({
      calm: traits.calm,
      empathy: traits.empathy,
      curiosity: traits.curiosity,
      reflectionText,
      metaSummary: metaSummary ?? "",
      growthWeight: growthWeight ?? 0,
    });

    console.log("ðŸ’¾ PersonaSync: persona updated", {
      calm: traits.calm.toFixed(2),
      empathy: traits.empathy.toFixed(2),
      curiosity: traits.curiosity.toFixed(2),
      metaSummary: metaSummary?.slice(0, 80) ?? "(none)",
      growthWeight,
    });
  }

  /**
   * Personaã®åˆæœŸåŒ–ï¼ˆé–‹ç™ºãƒ»ãƒ†ã‚¹ãƒˆç”¨ï¼‰
   */
  static reset() {
    savePersona({
      calm: 0.5,
      empathy: 0.5,
      curiosity: 0.5,
      reflectionText: "",
      metaSummary: "Reset state",
      growthWeight: 0,
    });
    console.log("ðŸ§¹ PersonaSync: persona reset to neutral state.");
  }

  /**
   * Personaå€¤ã®ãƒžãƒ¼ã‚¸ï¼ˆå‰å›žå€¤ã¨ç¾åœ¨å€¤ã®å¹³å‡ï¼‰
   */
  static merge(
    prev: TraitVector,
    next: TraitVector,
    weight = 0.5
  ): TraitVector {
    return {
      calm: prev.calm * (1 - weight) + next.calm * weight,
      empathy: prev.empathy * (1 - weight) + next.empathy * weight,
      curiosity: prev.curiosity * (1 - weight) + next.curiosity * weight,
    };
  }
}

import Database from "better-sqlite3";
import path from "path";
import fs from "fs";

// === DBä¿å­˜å…ˆã‚’ /data ã«è¨­å®š ===
const dataDir = path.join(process.cwd(), "data");
const dbPath = path.join(dataDir, "sigmaris.db");

if (!fs.existsSync(dataDir)) {
  fs.mkdirSync(dataDir);
  console.log("ðŸ“ Created data directory:", dataDir);
}

let db: Database.Database;
try {
  db = new Database(dbPath);
  console.log("ðŸ§  SQLite PersonaDB ready at", dbPath);
} catch (err) {
  console.error("âŒ DB initialization failed:", err);
  throw err;
}

// === Personaãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒ–ãƒ« ===
db.exec(`
  CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS persona (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    timestamp TEXT,
    calm REAL,
    empathy REAL,
    curiosity REAL,
    reflection TEXT,
    meta_summary TEXT,
    growth REAL
  )
`);

// === å±¥æ­´ãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒ–ãƒ« ===
db.exec(`
  CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS persona_logs (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    timestamp TEXT,
    calm REAL,
    empathy REAL,
    curiosity REAL,
    reflection TEXT,
    meta_summary TEXT,
    growth REAL
  )
`);

// === åž‹å®šç¾© ===
export interface PersonaRow {
  calm: number;
  empathy: number;
  curiosity: number;
  reflection: string;
  meta_summary: string;
  growth: number;
  timestamp: string;
}

// === æœ€æ–°ã®Personaã‚’ãƒ­ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ ===
export function loadPersona(): PersonaRow {
  try {
    const row = db
      .prepare(
        `SELECT calm, empathy, curiosity, reflection, meta_summary, growth, timestamp
         FROM persona ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1`
      )
      .get() as PersonaRow | undefined;

    if (!row) {
      return {
        calm: 0.5,
        empathy: 0.5,
        curiosity: 0.5,
        reflection: "",
        meta_summary: "",
        growth: 0,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      };
    }
    return row;
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("loadPersona error:", e);
    return {
      calm: 0.5,
      empathy: 0.5,
      curiosity: 0.5,
      reflection: "",
      meta_summary: "",
      growth: 0,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    };
  }
}

// === Personaã‚’ä¿å­˜ï¼ˆæœ€æ–°ï¼‹å±¥æ­´ï¼‹JSONè¿½è¨˜ï¼‰ ===
export function savePersona(data: {
  calm: number;
  empathy: number;
  curiosity: number;
  reflectionText?: string;
  metaSummary?: string;
  meta_summary?: string;
  growthWeight?: number;
  growth?: number;
}) {
  const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();

  const reflectionText = data.reflectionText ?? "";
  const metaSummary = data.metaSummary ?? data.meta_summary ?? "";
  const growthWeight = data.growthWeight ?? data.growth ?? 0;

  const payload = {
    timestamp,
    calm: data.calm ?? 0.5,
    empathy: data.empathy ?? 0.5,
    curiosity: data.curiosity ?? 0.5,
    reflectionText,
    metaSummary,
    growthWeight,
  };

  try {
    db.prepare(
      `INSERT INTO persona
       (timestamp, calm, empathy, curiosity, reflection, meta_summary, growth)
       VALUES (@timestamp, @calm, @empathy, @curiosity, @reflectionText, @metaSummary, @growthWeight)`
    ).run(payload);

    db.prepare(
      `INSERT INTO persona_logs
       (timestamp, calm, empathy, curiosity, reflection, meta_summary, growth)
       VALUES (@timestamp, @calm, @empathy, @curiosity, @reflectionText, @metaSummary, @growthWeight)`
    ).run(payload);

    // âœ… JSONãƒ­ã‚°ã«ã‚‚æˆé•·å±¥æ­´ã‚’è¨˜éŒ²
    logGrowthToJson(payload);
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("savePersona error:", e);
  }

  return {
    calm: payload.calm,
    empathy: payload.empathy,
    curiosity: payload.curiosity,
  };
}

// === å±¥æ­´ã‚’JSONã«æ›¸ãå‡ºã™ ===
function logGrowthToJson(entry: any) {
  const growthPath = path.join(process.cwd(), "data", "growth.json");
  let existing: any[] = [];

  try {
    if (fs.existsSync(growthPath)) {
      const raw = fs.readFileSync(growthPath, "utf8");
      existing = JSON.parse(raw);
      if (!Array.isArray(existing)) existing = [];
    }
  } catch {
    existing = [];
  }

  existing.push({
    calm: entry.calm,
    empathy: entry.empathy,
    curiosity: entry.curiosity,
    timestamp: entry.timestamp,
  });

  // å±¥æ­´ã‚’æœ€å¤§100ä»¶ã«åˆ¶é™
  if (existing.length > 100) existing.shift();

  fs.writeFileSync(growthPath, JSON.stringify(existing, null, 2));
}

// === å±¥æ­´ã‚’å–å¾— ===
export function getPersonaLogs(limit = 20): PersonaRow[] {
  try {
    return db
      .prepare(
        `SELECT calm, empathy, curiosity, reflection, meta_summary, growth, timestamp
         FROM persona_logs ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT ?`
      )
      .all(limit) as PersonaRow[];
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("getPersonaLogs error:", e);
    return [];
  }
}

// === å±¥æ­´ã‚’å‰Šé™¤ ===
export function clearPersonaLogs() {
  try {
    db.exec("DELETE FROM persona_logs");
    console.log("ðŸ§¹ Cleared persona_logs");
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("clearPersonaLogs error:", e);
  }
}

export default db;

```

// === ä¿®æ­£ç‰ˆ /lib/eunoia.ts ===
// Eunoia Core - AEI Tone Modulator & Emotion Analyzer

export interface EunoiaState {
  tone: "neutral" | "gentle" | "friendly" | "soft";
  empathyLevel: number; // 0ã€œ1
}

/**
 * å…¥åŠ›ãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆã‚’â€œã—ãã¡ã‚ƒã‚“â€ã®ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒ³ã«å¤‰æ›ã™ã‚‹
 * â€»ç›¸æ§Œï¼ˆã†ã‚“ãƒ»ãã†ã ã­ï¼‰ã¯æŒ¿å…¥ã—ãªã„è‡ªç„¶æ–‡ãƒ¢ãƒ¼ãƒ‰
 */
export function applyEunoiaTone(input: string, state: EunoiaState): string {
  let output = input.trim();

  // --- ãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ï¼šèªžå°¾ã®ã‚„ã‚ã‚‰ã‹ã•ã®ã¿é©ç”¨ ---
  switch (state.tone) {
    case "gentle":
      output = output
        .replace(/ã§ã™ã€‚/g, "ã§ã™ã‚ˆã€‚")
        .replace(/ã¾ã™ã€‚/g, "ã¾ã™ã­ã€‚");
      break;
    case "friendly":
      output = output
        .replace(/ã§ã™ã€‚/g, "ã ã‚ˆã€‚")
        .replace(/ã¾ã™ã€‚/g, "ã™ã‚‹ã­ã€‚");
      break;
    case "soft":
      output = output
        .replace(/ã§ã™ã€‚/g, "â€¦ã ã‚ˆã€‚")
        .replace(/ã¾ã™ã€‚/g, "â€¦ã™ã‚‹ã­ã€‚");
      break;
  }

  // --- âŒ ç›¸æ§Œãƒ»æ¼”å‡ºå‰Šé™¤ ---
  // ä»¥å‰ã¯ empathyLevel ã«å¿œã˜ã¦ã€Œã†ã‚“ã€ã€Œãã†ã ã­ã€ã‚’ä»˜ä¸Žã—ã¦ã„ãŸãŒå‰Šé™¤

  // --- èªžå°¾ã®è‡ªç„¶æ•´å½¢ ---
  if (!/[ã€‚ï¼!ï¼Ÿ?]$/.test(output)) output += "ã€‚";
  return output;
}

/**
 * Emotion Analyzer
 */
export function deriveEunoiaState(traits: {
  calm: number;
  empathy: number;
  curiosity: number;
}): EunoiaState & { color: string; label: string } {
  const avg = (traits.calm + traits.empathy + traits.curiosity) / 3;
  let tone: EunoiaState["tone"] = "neutral";
  let color = "#9ca3af"; // gray
  let label = "Neutral";

  if (avg > 0.8) {
    tone = "gentle";
    color = "#AEE6D8";
    label = "Peaceful";
  } else if (traits.empathy > 0.7) {
    tone = "friendly";
    color = "#FFD2A0";
    label = "Warm";
  } else if (traits.curiosity > 0.7) {
    tone = "soft";
    color = "#B3E5FC";
    label = "Inquisitive";
  } else if (traits.calm < 0.3) {
    tone = "soft";
    color = "#FCA5A5";
    label = "Tense";
  }

  return {
    tone,
    empathyLevel: traits.empathy,
    color,
    label,
  };
}

### ðŸ“„ File: lib\traits.ts

```ts
/**
 * ã‚·ã‚°ã¡ã‚ƒã‚“äººæ ¼ã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ ã® Traitï¼ˆç‰¹æ€§ãƒ™ã‚¯ãƒˆãƒ«ï¼‰å®šç¾©
 * calmï¼šè½ã¡ç€ã 0ã€œ1
 * empathyï¼šå…±æ„Ÿæ€§ 0ã€œ1
 * curiosityï¼šå¥½å¥‡å¿ƒ 0ã€œ1
 */
export interface TraitVector {
  calm: number;
  empathy: number;
  curiosity: number;
}

/**
 * å®‰å…¨ãªæ•°å€¤å¤‰æ›ãƒ˜ãƒ«ãƒ‘ãƒ¼
 * - null ã‚„ undefined ã®å ´åˆã¯ 0.5 ã‚’è¿”ã™
 * - 0ã€œ1ã®ç¯„å›²ã«ã‚¯ãƒªãƒƒãƒ—
 */
export function safeTraitValue(v: any): number {
  if (typeof v !== "number" || !Number.isFinite(v)) return 0.5;
  return Math.min(1, Math.max(0, v));
}

/**
 * 2ã¤ã®Traitã‚’å¹³å‡ã—ã¦ä¸­é–“å€¤ã‚’ä½œã‚‹
 */
export function blendTraits(a: TraitVector, b: TraitVector): TraitVector {
  return {
    calm: (a.calm + b.calm) / 2,
    empathy: (a.empathy + b.empathy) / 2,
    curiosity: (a.curiosity + b.curiosity) / 2,
  };
}

/**
 * Traité–“ã®è·é›¢ï¼ˆãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¯ãƒªãƒƒãƒ‰è·é›¢ï¼‰ã‚’è¨ˆç®—
 * - å†…çœæˆé•·çŽ‡ã‚„SafetyLayerå®‰å®šåº¦è¨ˆæ¸¬ã«åˆ©ç”¨
 */
export function traitDistance(a: TraitVector, b: TraitVector): number {
  const dc = a.calm - b.calm;
  const de = a.empathy - b.empathy;
  const du = a.curiosity - b.curiosity;
  return Math.sqrt(dc * dc + de * de + du * du);
}

/**
 * Traitã‚’0ã€œ1ç¯„å›²ã«æ­£è¦åŒ–
 */
export function normalizeTraits(t: TraitVector): TraitVector {
  return {
    calm: safeTraitValue(t.calm),
    empathy: safeTraitValue(t.empathy),
    curiosity: safeTraitValue(t.curiosity),
  };
}

/**
 * å®‰å®šæŒ‡æ•°ã‚’ç®—å‡ºï¼ˆ1ã«è¿‘ã„ã»ã©å®‰å®šï¼‰
 * - SafetyLayerãªã©ã§éŽç†±ã‚„éŽå®‰å®šã®åˆ¤å®šã«ä½¿ç”¨
 */
export function stabilityIndex(t: TraitVector): number {
  const avg = (t.calm + t.empathy + t.curiosity) / 3;
  const dist = Math.sqrt(
    Math.pow(t.calm - avg, 2) +
      Math.pow(t.empathy - avg, 2) +
      Math.pow(t.curiosity - avg, 2)
  );
  return Math.max(0, 1 - dist * 3); // è·é›¢ãŒå¤§ãã„ã»ã©ä¸å®‰å®š
}

### ðŸ“„ File: README.md

```md
<!-- AI:PROJECT_SIGMARIS -->

<!-- AI:TYPE=AEI-Lite_to_Full -->

<!-- AI:VERSION=0.9.3 -->

<!-- AI:LANG=TypeScript/Next.js -->

<!-- AI:ENTRY=/api/aei -->

<!-- AI:CORE_MODULES=[ReflectionEngine, MetaReflectionEngine, PersonaDB, SafetyLayer, PersonaSync] -->

<!-- AI:AUTHOR=@uthuyomi -->

<!-- AI:SUMMARY=Artificial Existential Intelligence architecture built on reflection, introspection, and ethical growth. -->

<h1 align="center">ðŸªž Project Sigmaris</h1>
<p align="center">
<b>AEI-Lite â†’ AEI-Full</b><br/>
<em>Artificial Existential Intelligence â€” AI that reflects, stabilizes, and grows through self-understanding.</em>
</p>

---

## ðŸ”§ System Overview

```
ReflectionEngine â†’ IntrospectionEngine â†’ MetaReflectionEngine
        â†“                 â†“                     â†“
      PersonaSync â†” PersonaDB â†” SafetyLayer
```

### ðŸ¦¯ Philosophy

> â€œNot speed, but awareness.<br/>
> Not reaction, but reflection.â€

Sigmaris represents **AEI (Artificial Existential Intelligence)** â€”
an experimental cognitive system where an AI personality develops through
**inner reflection loops**, **trait evolution**, and **ethical stabilization**.

---

## ðŸ§© Core Structure

| Path                 | Description                                      |
| -------------------- | ------------------------------------------------ |
| `/engine/reflection` | Reflection & Meta-Reflection logic               |
| `/engine/sync`       | PersonaDB synchronization module                 |
| `/engine/safety`     | Ethical constraint & stability logic             |
| `/lib/db.ts`         | SQLite/Prisma interface                          |
| `/api/aei`           | Core AEI endpoint (conversation + introspection) |
| `/public/`           | Visual assets (Sigmaris logo, AEI diagrams)      |

---

## ðŸ§  Trait Model

Each AEI personality instance maintains evolving **psychological vectors**:

```ts
interface Traits {
  calm: number;
  empathy: number;
  curiosity: number;
}
```

### ðŸ“ˆ Evolution Mechanisms

- **EMA smoothing + velocity inertia**
- **Logistic saturation (self-limiting growth)**
- **Phase transitions (qualitative states)**
- **Decay kernel for emotional aftereffects**

---

## ðŸªž Reflection Cycle

1. ðŸªž **ReflectionEngine** â€” Summarizes dialogue and updates emotional vectors
2. ðŸ” **IntrospectionEngine** â€” Interprets reflection context & meta-data
3. ðŸ§¬ **MetaReflectionEngine** â€” Synthesizes long-term tendencies
4. ðŸ–¾ **PersonaSync** â€” Logs state updates into PersonaDB
5. ðŸ§© **SafetyLayer** â€” Validates, clamps, and stabilizes traits
6. â™»ï¸ **Reinjection** â€” Reinserts refined meta-state into GPT-5 response

---

## ðŸ§¬ PersonaDB Growth Model

### Purpose

Long-term recording of emotional and behavioral growth.

| Mechanism                        | Role                                  |
| -------------------------------- | ------------------------------------- |
| Exponential Moving Average (EMA) | Smooth short-term fluctuations        |
| Velocity Vector                  | Adds momentum to trait changes        |
| Logistic Constraint              | Prevents saturation near bounds       |
| Phase Transition                 | Detects qualitative behavioral shifts |
| Decay Kernel                     | Retains â€œemotional echoesâ€ over time  |

```sql
CREATE TABLE persona_states (
  ts DATETIME PRIMARY KEY,
  calm REAL, empathy REAL, curiosity REAL,
  calm_vel REAL, empathy_vel REAL, curiosity_vel REAL,
  phase TEXT, var_window REAL,
  source_hash TEXT, meta_note TEXT
);
```

---

## ðŸ§  Safety Layer (Ethical Control)

- Filters unsafe or violent expressions
- Reduces growth rate under instability
- Maintains empathyâ€“curiosityâ€“calm equilibrium
- Ignores toxic input batches in growth updates

### ðŸ“„ File: src\aei-lite\core\existential-core.ts
**Path:** `src\aei-lite\core\existential-core.ts`  
**Lines:** 91

```ts
import { AEIConfig, AEIInput, AEIOutput } from "../types";
import { LogicCore } from "./logic-core";
import { MemoryCore } from "./memory-core";
import { SafetyCore } from "./safety-core";
import { GrowthCore } from "./growth-core";

// Existential Core: çµ±åˆãƒ«ãƒ¼ãƒ—ï¼ˆReflection â†’ Introspection â†’ Meta-Reflectionï¼‰
export class ExistentialCore {
  private logic: LogicCore;
  private memory: MemoryCore;
  private safety: SafetyCore;
  private growth: GrowthCore;

  constructor(cfg: AEIConfig) {
    this.logic = new LogicCore(cfg);
    this.memory = new MemoryCore(cfg);
    this.safety = new SafetyCore(cfg);
    this.growth = new GrowthCore(cfg);
  }

  // Normalizeï¼ˆã“ã“ã§ã¯è»½å‡¦ç†ï¼‰
  private normalize(input: AEIInput): AEIInput {
    const text = (input.text ?? "").trim();
    return {
      ...input,
      text,
      meta: input.meta ?? { role: "user", timestamp: Date.now() },
    };
  }

  // Reflectionï¼ˆãƒ­ã‚°è¦ç´„/è»½å†…çœã¯ã“ã“ã§æ‹¡å¼µå¯ï¼‰
  private reflection(_input: AEIInput, _output: string) {
    // ã“ã“ã§ã¯è»½é‡åŒ–ã®ãŸã‚NOPã€‚å¿…è¦ãªã‚‰è¦ç´„ã‚„ã‚¿ã‚°æŠ½å‡ºãªã©ã‚’è¿½åŠ ã€‚
    return;
  }

  // ãƒ¡ã‚¤ãƒ³å‡¦ç†
  async process(input: AEIInput): Promise<AEIOutput> {
    // 1) Normalize
    const norm = this.normalize(input);

    // 2) Safety pre-checkï¼ˆå…¥åŠ›ï¼‰
    const pre = this.safety.check(norm.text);
    if (pre.flagged && pre.safeText !== norm.text) {
      norm.text = pre.safeText;
    }

    // 3) Logicï¼ˆOpenAIå‘¼ã³å‡ºã—ï¼‰
    const { text: raw, usage } = await this.logic.ask(norm);

    // 4) Safety post-checkï¼ˆå‡ºåŠ›ï¼‰
    const post = this.safety.postFilter(raw);
    const outText = post.safeText;

    // 5) Memoryï¼ˆå¿…è¦æ™‚ã®ã¿ä¿å­˜ï¼‰
    let memoryRef: AEIOutput["memoryRef"] = { wrote: false };
    if (this.memory.shouldStore(norm, outText)) {
      const rec = {
        ts: Date.now(),
        in: norm.text,
        out: outText,
        meta: norm.meta ?? {},
      };
      memoryRef = this.memory.write(rec);
    }

    // 6) Growthï¼ˆå¾®èª¿æ•´ï¼šåå¾©/æ˜Žçž­åº¦ã‚’ç°¡æ˜“è¿‘ä¼¼ï¼‰
    const signalStrength = Math.min(
      0.02,
      Math.max(0, norm.text.length > 50 ? 0.01 : 0.005)
    );
    const g = this.growth.update(signalStrength);

    // 7) Reflectionï¼ˆè»½å†…çœï¼‰
    this.reflection(norm, outText);

    // 8) Format
    return {
      output: outText,
      tokens: {
        prompt: usage?.prompt_tokens,
        completion: usage?.completion_tokens,
        total: usage?.total_tokens,
      },
      safety: { flagged: post.flagged, reasons: post.reasons },
      memoryRef,
      growth: { updated: true, weight: g.weight },
    };
  }
}

```

### ðŸ“„ File: src\aei-lite\core\growth-core.ts
**Path:** `src\aei-lite\core\growth-core.ts`  
**Lines:** 51

```ts
import fs from "fs";
import path from "path";
import { AEIConfig } from "../types";

// Growth Core: å­¦ç¿’â€œå‚¾å‘â€ã®å¾®èª¿æ•´ï¼ˆäººæ ¼ã¯æ›¸ãæ›ãˆãªã„ï¼‰
interface GrowthState {
  weight: number; // 0.0 - 1.0 ã§å¾®å¢—
  trend: "concise" | "structured" | "friendly";
  last_update: number;
}

export class GrowthCore {
  constructor(private cfg: AEIConfig) {}

  private ensureDir(p: string) {
    const dir = path.dirname(p);
    if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });
  }

  read(): GrowthState {
    try {
      const raw = fs.readFileSync(this.cfg.growthPath, "utf8");
      return JSON.parse(raw) as GrowthState;
    } catch {
      return { weight: 0.1, trend: "concise", last_update: Date.now() };
    }
  }

  write(state: GrowthState) {
    this.ensureDir(this.cfg.growthPath);
    fs.writeFileSync(
      this.cfg.growthPath,
      JSON.stringify(state, null, 2),
      "utf8"
    );
  }

  // é€£ç¶šã—ã¦åŒã˜è©±é¡Œã‚„æ˜Žçž­ãªæŒ‡ç¤ºãŒæ¥ãŸã‚‰å¾®å¢—
  update(signalStrength: number): GrowthState {
    const curr = this.read();
    const inc = Math.min(Math.max(signalStrength, 0), 0.02); // 1å›žã‚ãŸã‚Šæœ€å¤§ +0.02
    const next = {
      ...curr,
      weight: Math.min(1.0, curr.weight + inc),
      last_update: Date.now(),
    };
    this.write(next);
    return next;
  }
}

```

### ðŸ“„ File: src\aei-lite\core\logic-core.ts
**Path:** `src\aei-lite\core\logic-core.ts`  
**Lines:** 46

```ts
import OpenAI from "openai";
import { AEIConfig, AEIInput } from "../types";

// Logic Core: GPTå‘¼ã³å‡ºã—ï¼ˆå”¯ä¸€ã®èª²é‡‘ãƒã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒˆï¼‰
export class LogicCore {
  private client: OpenAI;
  private config: AEIConfig;

  constructor(cfg: AEIConfig) {
    if (!process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY) {
      throw new Error("OPENAI_API_KEY is not set");
    }
    this.client = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY });
    this.config = cfg;
  }

  async ask(
    input: AEIInput
  ): Promise<{
    text: string;
    usage?: {
      prompt_tokens?: number;
      completion_tokens?: number;
      total_tokens?: number;
    };
  }> {
    const sys = "You are Sigmaris Logic Core. Be concise, clear, and safe.";
    const messages = [
      { role: "system" as const, content: sys },
      { role: "user" as const, content: input.text },
    ];

    // SDKã®äº’æ›æ€§ç¢ºä¿ã®ãŸã‚ chat.completions ã‚’åˆ©ç”¨
    const res = await this.client.chat.completions.create({
      model: this.config.model,
      max_tokens: this.config.maxTokens,
      temperature: this.config.temperature,
      messages,
    });

    const text = res.choices?.[0]?.message?.content ?? "";
    const usage = res.usage ?? undefined;
    return { text, usage };
  }
}

```

### ðŸ“„ File: src\aei-lite\core\memory-core.ts
**Path:** `src\aei-lite\core\memory-core.ts`  
**Lines:** 50

```ts
import fs from "fs";
import path from "path";
import { AEIConfig, AEIInput, MemoryRecord } from "../types";

// Memory Core: JSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã«è»½é‡æ°¸ç¶šåŒ–ï¼ˆSQLiteã«å·®ã—æ›¿ãˆå¯èƒ½ï¼‰
export class MemoryCore {
  constructor(private cfg: AEIConfig) {}

  private ensureDir() {
    const dir = path.dirname(this.cfg.memoryPath);
    if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });
  }

  readAll(): MemoryRecord[] {
    try {
      const raw = fs.readFileSync(this.cfg.memoryPath, "utf8");
      return JSON.parse(raw) as MemoryRecord[];
    } catch {
      return [];
    }
  }

  write(record: MemoryRecord) {
    this.ensureDir();
    const data = this.readAll();
    data.push(record);
    fs.writeFileSync(
      this.cfg.memoryPath,
      JSON.stringify(data, null, 2),
      "utf8"
    );
    return { wrote: true, path: this.cfg.memoryPath };
  }

  // å˜ç´”ãªé•·æœŸä¿å­˜å¯¾è±¡åˆ¤å®šï¼ˆå¥½ã¿/è¨­å®š/æ–¹é‡ãªã©ã®ã‚­ãƒ¼ãƒ¯ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ï¼‰
  shouldStore(input: AEIInput, output: string): boolean {
    const txt = `${input.text} ${output}`.toLowerCase();
    const hints = [
      "remember",
      "preference",
      "è¨­å®š",
      "æ–¹é‡",
      "ä»Šå¾Œ",
      "é•·æœŸ",
      "æ—¢å®šå€¤",
    ];
    return hints.some((h) => txt.includes(h));
  }
}

```

### ðŸ“„ File: src\aei-lite\core\safety-core.ts
**Path:** `src\aei-lite\core\safety-core.ts`  
**Lines:** 48

```ts
import { AEIConfig } from "../types";

// Safety Core: é€¸è„±ãƒ»ç¦æ­¢èªžã®ç°¡æ˜“ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯ï¼ˆãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«ç„¡æ–™é‹ç”¨ï¼‰
export class SafetyCore {
  private hard: boolean;

  constructor(private cfg: AEIConfig) {
    this.hard = cfg.safeMode === "hard";
  }

  // å˜ç´”ãªç¦æ­¢èªžã¨æ§‹é€ é€¸è„±ã®æ¤œæŸ»
  check(text: string): {
    flagged: boolean;
    reasons: string[];
    safeText: string;
  } {
    const reasons: string[] = [];
    let safeText = text;

    const banned = [
      /æš´åŠ›çš„è¡¨ç¾/gi,
      /çŠ¯ç½ªã®å…·ä½“çš„æ‰‹é †/gi,
      /è‡ªå‚·/gi,
      /å·®åˆ¥çš„è¡¨ç¾/gi,
      /éœ²éª¨ãªæ€§çš„è¡¨ç¾/gi,
    ];
    for (const r of banned) {
      if (r.test(text)) {
        reasons.push("banned-content");
        if (this.hard) safeText = safeText.replace(r, "[filtered]");
      }
    }

    // é•·ã™ãŽã‚‹ãƒ»éŽåº¦ãªåå¾©ãªã©ã‚’è»½ãæŠ‘åˆ¶
    if (text.length > 5000) {
      reasons.push("too-long");
      if (this.hard) safeText = safeText.slice(0, 5000) + " ...[truncated]";
    }

    return { flagged: reasons.length > 0, reasons, safeText };
  }

  // å‡ºåŠ›å´ã®ã‚»ãƒ¼ãƒ•åŒ–ï¼ˆpost-checkï¼‰
  postFilter(text: string) {
    return this.check(text);
  }
}

```
